nirvikalpāḥ sadā yuktāścittacaittavivarjitāḥ  Lank 
balābhijñāvaśiprāptāḥ tatsamādhigatiṃgatāḥ 
tatra budhyanti saṃbuddhā nirmitastviha budhyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
nirmāṇakoṭyo hyamitā buddhānāṃ niścaranti ca 
sarvatra bālāḥ śṛṇvanti dharmaṃ tebhyaḥ pratiśrutvā   Lank 
ādimadhyāntanirmuktaṃ bhāvābhāvavivarjitam 
vyāpinamacalaṃ śuddhamacitraṃ citrasaṃbhavam  Lank 
vijñaptigotrasaṃchannamālīnaṃ sarvadehinām 
bhrānteśca vidyate māyā na māyā bhrāntikāraṇam  Lank 
cittasya mohenāpyasti yatkiṃcidapi vidyate 
svabhāvadvayanibaddhamālayavijñānanirmitam 
lokaṃ vijñaptimātraṃ ca dṛṣṭyaughaṃ dharmapudgalam  Lank 
vibhāvya lokamevaṃ tu parāvṛtto yadā bhavet 
tadā putro bhavenmahyaṃ niṣpannadharmavartakaḥ  Lank 
uṣṇadravacalakaṭhinā dharmā bālairvikalpitāḥ 
asadbhūtasamāropo nāsti lakṣyaṃ na lakṣaṇam  Lank 
aṣṭadravyakametattu kāyasaṃsthānamindriyam 
rūpaṃ kalpanti vai bālā bhrāntāḥ saṃsārapañjare  Lank 
hetupratyayasāmagryā bālāḥ kalpanti saṃbhavam 
ajānānā nayamidaṃ bhramanti tribhavālaye  Lank 
sarvabhāvāsvabhāvā ca vacanamapi nṛṇām 
kalpanāccāpi nirmāṇaṃ nāsti svapnopamaṃ bhavam 
parīkṣenna saṃsarennāpi nirvāyāt  Lank 
cittaṃ vicitraṃ bījākhyaṃ khyāyate cittagocaram 
khyātau kalpanti utpattiṃ bālāḥ kalpadvaye ratāḥ  Lank 
ajñāna tṛṣṇā karmaṃ ca cittacaittā na mārakam 
pravartati tato yasmātpāratantryaṃ hi tanmatam  Lank 
te ca kalpanti yadvastu cittagocaravibhramam 
kalpanāyāmaniṣpannaṃ mithyābhrāntivikalpitam  Lank 
cittaṃ pratyayasaṃbaddhaṃ pravartati śarīriṇām 
pratyayebhyo vinirmuktaṃ na paśyāmi vadāmyaham  Lank 
pratyayebhyo vinirmuktaṃ svalakṣaṇavivarjitam 
na tiṣṭhati yadā dehe tena mahyamagocaram  Lank 
Vaidya 
rājā śreṣṭhī yathā putrān vicitrairmṛgasādṛśaiḥ 
pralobhya krīḍati gṛhe vane mṛgasamāgamam  Lank 
tathāhaṃ lakṣaṇaiścitrairdharmāṇāṃ pratibimbakaiḥ 
pratyātmavedyāṃ hi sutāṃ bhūtakoṭiṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
taraṃgā hyudadheryadvatpavanapratyayoditāḥ 
nṛtyamānāḥ pravartante vyucchedaścaḥ na vidyate  Lank 
ālayaughastathā nityaṃ viṣayapavaneritaḥ 
citraistaraṃgavijñānairnṛtyamānaḥ pravartate  Lank 
grāhyagrāhakabhāvena cittaṃ namati dehinām 
dṛśyasya lakṣaṇaṃ nāsti yathā bālairvikalpyate  Lank 
paramālayavijñānaṃ vijñaptirālayaṃ punaḥ 
grāhyagrāhakāpagamāttathatāṃ deśayāmyaham  Lank 
nāsti skandheṣvātmā na sattvo na ca pudgalaḥ 
utpadyate ca vijñānaṃ vijñānaṃ ca nirudhyate  Lank 
nimnonnataṃ yathā citre dṛśyate na ca vidyate 
tathā bhāveṣu bhāvatvaṃ dṛśyate na ca vidyate  Lank 
gandharvanagaraṃ yadvadyathā ca mṛgatṛṣṇikā 
dṛśyaṃ khyāti tathā nityaṃ prajñayā ca na vidyate  Lank 
pramāṇendriyanirvṛttaṃ na kāryaṃ nāpi kāraṇam 
buddhiboddhavyarahitaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam  Lank 
skandhān pratītya saṃbuddho na dṛṣṭaḥ kenacitkvacit 
yo na dṛṣṭaḥ kvacitkena kutastasya vibhāvanā  Lank 
pratyayairhetudṛṣṭāntaiḥ pratijñā kāraṇena ca 
svapnagandharvacakreṇa marīcyā somabhāskaraiḥ  Lank 
adṛśyaṃ kulādidṛṣṭāntairutpattiṃ vādayāmyaham 
svapnavibhramamāyākhyaṃ śūnyaṃ vai kalpitaṃ jagat  Lank 
anāśritaśca trailokye adhyātmaṃ ca bahistathā 
anutpannaṃ bhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣāntyanutpatti jāyate  Lank 
māyopamasamādhiṃ ca kāyaṃ manomayaṃ punaḥ 
abhijñā vaśitā tasya balā cittasya citritā  Lank 
bhāvā yeṣāṃ hyanutpannāḥ śūnyā vai asvabhāvakāḥ 
teṣāmutpadyate bhrāntiḥ pratyayaiśca nirudhyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
cittaṃ hi khyāti cittasya bahirdhā khyāti rūpiṇaḥ 
anyanna vidyate dṛśyaṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate  Lank 
saṃkalā buddhabimbaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ ca vidāraṇam 
adhiṣṭhanti jagaccitraṃ prajñaptyā vai suśikṣitāḥ  Lank 
dehaḥ pratiṣṭhā bhogaśca grāhyavijñaptayastrayaḥ 
mana udgrahavijñaptivikalpo grāhakāstrayaḥ  Lank 
vikalpaśca vikalpyaṃ ca yāvattvakṣaragocaram 
tāvattattvaṃ na paśyanti tārkikāstarkavibhramāt  Lank 
naiḥsvabhāvyaṃ hi bhāvānāṃ yadā budhyanti prajñayā 
tadā viśramati yogī ānimittapratiṣṭhitaḥ  Lank 
masimrakṣitako yadvadgṛhyate kurkuṭo 'budhaiḥ 
sa evāyamajānānairbālairyānatrayaṃ tathā  Lank 
na hyatra śrāvakāḥ kecinnāsti pratyekayānikāḥ 
yaccaitaddṛśyate rūpaṃ śrāvakasya jinasya ca 
nirmāṇaṃ deśayantyete bodhisattvāḥ kṛpātmakāḥ  Lank 
vijñaptimātraṃ tribhavaṃ svabhāvadvayakalpitam 
parāvṛttastu tathatā dharmapudgalasaṃcarāt  Lank 
somabhāskaradīpārcirbhūtāni maṇayastathā 
nirvikalpāḥ pravartante tathā buddhasya buddhatā  Lank 
keśoṇḍukaṃ yathā mithyā gṛhyate taimirairjanaiḥ 
tathā bhāvavikalpo 'yaṃ mithyā bālairvikalpyate  Lank 
sthitibhaṅgotpattirahitā nityānityavivarjitāḥ 
saṃkleśavyavadānākhyā bhāvāḥ keśoṇḍukopamāḥ  Lank 
puttalikaṃ yathā kaścitkanakābhaṃ paśyate jagat 
na hyasti kanakaṃ tatra bhūmiśca kanakāyate  Lank 
evaṃ hi dūṣitā bālāścittacaittairanādikaiḥ 
māyāmarīciprabhavaṃ bhāvaṃ gṛhṇanti tattvataḥ  Lank 
ekabījamabījaṃ ca samudraikaṃ ca bījakam 
sarvabījakamapyetaccittaṃ paśyatha citrikam  Lank 
ekaṃ bījaṃ yadā śuddhaṃ parāvṛttamabījakam 
samaṃ hi nirvikalpatvādudrekājjanmasaṃkaraḥ 
bījamāvahate citraṃ sarvabījaṃ taducyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
na hyatrotpadyate kiṃcitpratyayairna nirudhyate 
utpadyante nirudhyante pratyayā eva kalpitāḥ  Lank 
prajñaptimātraṃ tribhavaṃ nāsti vastu svabhāvataḥ 
prajñaptivastubhāvena kalpayiṣyanti tārkikāḥ  Lank 
bhāvasvabhāvajijñāsā na hi bhrāntirnivāryate 
bhāvasvabhāvānutpattirevaṃ dṛṣṭvā vimucyate  Lank 
na māyā nāstisādharmyādbhāvānāṃ kathyate 'stitā 
vitathāśuvidyutsadṛśāstena māyopamāḥ smṛtāḥ  Lank 
na cotpadyā na cotpannāḥ pratyayo 'pi na kecana 
saṃvidyante kvacittena vyavahāraṃ tu kathyate  Lank 
na bhaṅgotpādasaṃkleśaḥ pratyayānāṃ nivāryate 
yattu bālā vikalpenti pratyayaiḥ saṃnivāryate  Lank 
na svabhāvo na vijñaptirna vastu na ca ālayaḥ 
bālairvikalpitā hyete vaśabhūtaiḥ kutārkikaiḥ  Lank 
cittamātraṃ yadā lokaṃ prapaśyanti jinātmajāḥ 
tadā nairvāṇikaṃ kāyaṃ kriyāsaṃskāravarjitam 
labhante te balābhijñāvaśitaiḥ saha saṃyutam  Lank 
sarvarūpāvabhāsaṃ hi yadā cittaṃ pravartate 
nātra cittaṃ na rūpāṇi bhrāntaṃ cittamanādikam  Lank 
tadā yogī hyanābhāsaṃ prajñayā paśyate jagat 
nimittaṃ vastuvijñaptirmanovispanditaṃ ca yat 
atikramya tu putrā me nirvikalpāścaranti te  Lank 
gandharvanagaraṃ māyā keśoṇḍuka marīcikā 
asatyāḥ satyataḥ khyānti tathā bhāveṣu bhāvanā  Lank 
anutpannāḥ sarvabhāvā bhrāntimātraṃ hi dṛśyate 
bhrāntiṃ kalpenti utpannāṃ bālāṃ kalpadvaye ratāḥ  Lank 
aupapattyaṅgikaṃ cittaṃ vicitraṃ vāsanāsaṃbhavam 
pravartate taraṃgaughaṃ tacchedānna pravartate  Lank 
vicitrālambanaṃ citraṃ yathā citte pravatate 
tathākāśe ca kuḍye ca kasmānnābhipravartate  Lank 
nimitaṃ kiṃcidālambya yadi cittaṃ pravartate 
pratyayairjanitaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
cittena gṛhyate cittaṃ nāsti kiṃcitsahetukam 
cittasya dharmatā śuddhā gagane nāsti vāsanā  Lank 
svacittābhiniveśena cittaṃ vai saṃpravartate 
bahirdhā nāsti vai dṛśyamato vai cittamātrakam  Lank 
cittamālayavijñānaṃ mano yanmanyanātmakam 
gṛhṇāti viṣayān yena vijñānaṃ hi taducyate  Lank 
cittamavyākṛtaṃ nityaṃ mano hyubhayasaṃcaram 
vartamānaṃ hi vijñānaṃ kuśalākuśalaṃ hi tat  Lank 
dvāraṃ hi paramārthasya vijñaptidvayavarjitam 
yānatrayavyavasthānaṃ nirābhāse sthitaṃ kutaḥ  Lank 
cittamātraṃ nirābhāsaṃ vihārā buddhabhūmiśca 
etaddhi bhāṣitaṃ buddhairbhāṣante bhāṣayanti ca  Lank 
cittaṃ hi bhūmayaḥ sapta nirābhāsā ca aṣṭamī 
dve bhūmayo vihāraśca śeṣā bhūmirmamātmikā  Lank 
pratyātmavedyā śuddhā ca bhūmiścāpi mamātmikā 
māheśvaraparasthānamakaniṣṭhe virājate  Lank 
hutāśanasyaiva yathā niścerustasya raśmayaḥ 
citrā manoharāḥ saumyāstribhavaṃ nirmiṇanti ye  Lank 
nirmāya tribhavaṃ kiṃcitkiṃcidvai pūrvanirmitam 
tatra deśanti yānāni eṣā bhūmirmamātmikā  Lank 
nāsti kālo hyadhigame bhūmīnāṃ kṣatresaṃkrame 
cittamātramatikramya nirābhāse sthitaṃ phalam  Lank 
asattā caiva sattā ca dṛśyate ca vicitratā 
bālā grāhaviparyastā viparyāso hi citratā  Lank 
nirvikalpaṃ yadi jñānaṃ vastvastīti na yujyate 
yasmāccittaṃ na rūpāṇi nirvikalpaṃ hi tena tat  Lank 
indriyāṇi ca māyākhyā viṣayāḥ svapnasaṃnibhāḥ 
kartā karma kriyā caiva sarvathāpi na vidyate  Lank 
dhyānāni cāpramāṇāni ārūpyāśca samādhayaḥ 
saṃjñānirodho nikhilaścittamātre na vidyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
srotāpattiphalaṃ caiva sakṛdāgāmiphalaṃ tathā 
anāgāmiphalaṃ caiva arhattvaṃ cittavibhramaḥ  Lank 
śūnyamanityaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ bālāḥ kalpanti saṃskṛtam 
nadīdīpādidṛṣṭāntaiḥ kṣaṇikārtho vikalpyate  Lank 
nirvyāpāraṃ tu kṣaṇikaṃ viviktaṃ kriyavarjitam 
anutpattiṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ kṣaṇikārthaṃ vadāmyahyam  Lank 
saccāsato hyanutpādaḥ sāṃkhyavaiśeṣikaiḥ smṛtaḥ 
avyākṛtāni sarvāṇi taireva hi prakāśitam  Lank 
caturvidhaṃ vyākaraṇamekāṃśaparipṛcchanam 
vibhajyasthāpanīyaṃ ca tīrthavādanivāraṇam  Lank 
sarvaṃ vidyati saṃvṛtyāṃ paramārthe na vidyate 
dharmāṇāṃ niḥsvabhāvatvaṃ paramārthe 'pi dṛśyate 
upalabdhiniḥsvabhāve saṃvṛtistena ucyate  Lank 
abhilāpahetuko bhāvaḥ svabhāvo yadi vidyate 
abhilāpasaṃbhavo bhāvo nāstīti ca na vidyate  Lank 
nirvastuko hyabhilāpastatsaṃvṛtyāpi na vidyate 
viparyāsasya vastutvāccopalabdhirna vidyate  Lank 
vidyate cedviparyāso naiḥsvābhāvyaṃ na vidyate 
viparyāsasya vastutvādyadyadevopalabhyate 
niḥsvabhāvaṃ bhavettaddhi sarvathāpi na vidyate  Lank 
yadetaddṛśyate citraṃ cittaṃ dauṣṭhulyavāsitam 
rūpāvabhāsagrahaṇaṃ bahirdhā cittavibhramam  Lank 
vikalpenāvikalpena vikalpo hi prahīyate 
vikalpenāvikalpena śūnyatātattvadarśanam  Lank 
māyāhastī yathā citraṃ patrāṇi kanakā yathā 
tathā dṛśyaṃ nṛṇāṃ khyāti citte ajñānavāsite  Lank 
āryo na paśyate bhrāntiṃ nāpi tattvaṃ tadantare 
bhrāntireva bhavettattvaṃ yasmāttattvaṃ tadantare  Lank 
bhrāntiṃ vidhūya sarvāṃ tu nimittaṃ yadi jāyate 
saiva cāsya bhavedbhrāntiraśuddhaṃ timiraṃ yathā  Lank 
keśoṇḍukaṃ taimiriko yathā gṛhṇāti vibhramāt 
viṣayeṣu tadvadbālānāṃ grahaṇaṃ saṃpravartate  Lank 
Vaidya 
keśoṇḍukaprakhyamidaṃ marīcyudakavibhramam 
tribhavaṃ svapnamāyābhaṃ vibhāvento vimucyate  Lank 
vikalpaśca vikalpyaśca vikalpasya pravartate 
bandho bandhyaśca baddhaśca ṣaḍete mokṣahetavaḥ  Lank 
na bhūmayo na satyāni na kṣetrā na ca nirmitāḥ 
buddhāḥ pratyekabuddhāśca śrāvakāścāpi kalpitāḥ  Lank 
pudgalaḥ saṃtatiḥ skandhāḥ pratyayā hyaṇavastathā 
pradhānamīśvaraḥ kartā cittamātre vikalpyate  Lank 
cittaṃ hi sarvaṃ sarvatra sarvadeheṣu vartate 
vicitraṃ gṛhyate 'sadbhiścittamātraṃ hyalakṣaṇam  Lank 
na hyātmā vidyate skandhe skandhāścaiva hi nātmani 
na te yathā vikalpyante na ca te vai na santi ca  Lank 
astitvaṃ sarvabhāvānāṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate 
yadi te bhavedyathādṛṣṭāḥ sarve syustattvadarśinaḥ  Lank 
abhāvātsarvadharmaṇāṃ saṃkleśo nāsti śuddhi ca 
na ca te tathā yathādṛṣṭā na ca te vai na santi ca  Lank 
bhrāntirnimittaṃ saṃkalpaḥ paratantrasya lakṣaṇam 
tasminnimitte yannāma tadvikalpitalakṣaṇam  Lank 
nāmanimittasaṃkalpo yadā tasya na jāyate 
pratyayāvastusaṃketaṃ pariniṣpannalakṣaṇam  Lank 
vaipākikāśca ye buddhā jinā nairmāṇikāśca ye 
sattvāśca bodhisattvāśca kṣetrāṇi ca diśe diśe  Lank 
nisyandadharmanirmāṇā jinā nairmāṇikāśca ye 
sarve te hyamitābhasya sukhāvatyā vinirgatāḥ  Lank 
yacca nairmāṇikairbhāṣṭaṃ yacca bhāṣṭaṃ vipākajaiḥ 
sūtrāntavaipulyanayaṃ tasya saṃdhiṃ vijānatha  Lank 
yadbhāṣitaṃ jinasutairyacca bhāṣanti nāyakāḥ 
yaddhi nairmāṇikābhāṣṭaṃ na tu vaipākikairjinaiḥ  Lank 
anutpannā hyamī dharmā na caivaite na santi ca 
gandharvanagarasvapnamāyānirmāṇasādṛśāḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
cittaṃ pravartate cittaṃ cittameva vimucyate 
cittaṃ hi jāyate nānyaccittameva nirudhyate  Lank 
arthābhāsaṃ nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ cittaṃ vai khyāti kalpitam 
nāstyarthaścittamātreyaṃ nirvikalpo vimucyate  Lank 
anādikālaprapañcadauṣṭhulyaṃ hi samāhitam 
vikalpo bhāvitastena mithyābhāsaṃ pravartate  Lank 
arthābhāse ca vijñāne jñānaṃ tathatāgocaram 
parāvṛttaṃ nirābhāsamāryāṇāṃ gocare hyasau  Lank 
arthapravicayaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyānaṃ bālopacārikam 
tathatārambaṇaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyānaṃ tāthāgataṃ śubham  Lank 
parikalpitaṃ svabhāvena sarvadharmā ajānakāḥ 
paratantraṃ samāśritya vikalpo bhramate nṛṇām  Lank 
paratantraṃ yathā śuddhaṃ vikalpena visaṃyutam 
parāvṛttaṃ hi tathatā vihāraḥ kalpavarjitaḥ  Lank 
mā vikalpaṃ vikalpetha vikalpo nāsti satyataḥ 
bhrāntiṃ vikalpayantasya grāhyagrāhakayorna tu 
bāhyārthadarśanaṃ kalpaṃ svabhāvaḥ parikalpitaḥ  Lank 
yena kalpena kalpenti svabhāvaḥ pratyayodbhavaḥ 
bāhyārthadarśanaṃ mithyā nāstyarthaṃ cittameva tu  Lank 
yuktyā vipaśyamānānāṃ grāhagrāhyaṃ nirudhyate 
bāhyo na vidyate hyartho yathā bālairvikalpyate  Lank 
vāsanairlulitaṃ cittamarthābhāsaṃ pravartate 
kalpadvayanirodhena jñānaṃ tathatagocaram  Lank 
utpadyate hyanābhāsamacintyamāryagocaram 
nāmanimittasaṃkalpaḥ svabhāvadvayalakṣaṇam 
samyagjñānaṃ hi tathatā pariniṣpannalakṣaṇam  Lank 
mātāpitṛsamāyogādālayamanasaṃyutam 
ghṛtakumbhe mūṣikā yadvatsaha śukreṇa vardhate  Lank 
peśīghanārbudaṃ piṭakamaśubhaṃ karmacitritam 
karmavāyumahābhūtaiḥ phalavatsaṃprapadyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
pañcapañcakapañcaiva vraṇāścaiva navaiva tu 
nakhadantaromasaṃchannaḥ sphuramāṇaḥ prajāyate  Lank 
prajātamātraṃ viṣṭhākṛmiṃ suptabuddheva mānavaḥ 
cakṣuṣā sphurate rūpaṃ vivṛddhiṃ yāti kalpanāt  Lank 
tālvoṣṭhapuṭasaṃyogādvikalpenāvadhāryate 
vācā pravartate nṝṇāṃ śukasyeva vikalpanā  Lank 
niścitāstīrthyavādānāṃ mahāyānamaniścitam 
sattvāśrayapravṛtto 'yaṃ kudṛṣṭīnāmanāspadam  Lank 
pratyātmavedyayānaṃ me tārkikāṇāmagocaram 
paścātkāle gate nāthe brūhi ko 'yaṃ dhariṣyati  Lank 
nirvṛte sugate paścātkālo 'tīto bhaviṣyati 
mahāmate nibodha tvaṃ yo netrīṃ dhārayiṣyati  Lank 
dakṣiṇāpathavedalyāṃ bhikṣuḥ śrīmān mahāyaśāḥ 
nāgāhvayaḥ sa nāmnā tu sadasatpakṣadārakaḥ  Lank 
prakāśya loke madyānaṃ mahāyānamanuttaram 
āsādya bhūmiṃ muditāṃ yāsyate 'sau sukhāvatīm  Lank 
buddhyā vivecyamānānāṃ svabhāvo nāvadhāryate 
yasmāttadanabhilāpyāste niḥsvabhāvāśca deśitāḥ  Lank 
pratyayotpādite hyarthe nāstyastīti na vidyate 
pratyayāntargataṃ bhāvaṃ ye kalpentyasti nāsti ca 
dūrībhūtā bhavenmanye śāsanāttīrthadṛṣṭayaḥ  Lank 
abhidhānaṃ sarvabhāvānāṃ janmāntaraśataiḥ sadā 
abhyastamabhyasantaṃ ca parasparavikalpayā  Lank 
akathyamāne saṃmohaṃ sarvaloka āpadyate 
tasmātkriyate nāma saṃmohasya vyudāsārtham  Lank 
trividhena vikalpena bālairbhāvā vikalpitāḥ 
bhrāntirnāmavikalpena pratyayairjanitena ca  Lank 
aniruddhā hyanutpannāḥ prakṛtyā gaganopamāḥ 
abhāvasvabhāvā ye tu te vikalpitalakṣaṇāḥ  Lank 
pratibhāsabimbamāyābhamarīcyā supinena tu 
alātacakragandharvapratiśrutkāsamodbhavāḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
advayā tathatā śūnyā bhūtakoṣṭiśca dharmatā 
nirvikalpaśca deśemi ye te niṣpannalakṣaṇāḥ  Lank 
vākcittagocaraṃ mithyā satyaṃ prajñā vikalpitā 
dvayāntapatitaṃ cittaṃ tasmātprajñā na kalpitā  Lank 
asti nāsti ca dvāvantau yāvaccittasya gocaraḥ 
gocareṇa vidhūtena samyakcittaṃ nirudhyate  Lank 
viṣayagrahaṇābhāvānnirodhena ca nāsti ca 
vidyate tathatāvasthā āryāṇāṃ gocaro yathā  Lank 
bālānāṃ na tathā khyāti yathā khyāti manīṣiṇām 
manīṣiṇāṃ tathā khyāti sarvadharmā alakṣaṇāḥ  Lank 
hārakūṭaṃ yathā bālaiḥ suvarṇaṃ parikalpyate 
asuvarṇaṃ suvarṇābhaṃ tathā dharmāḥ kutārkikaiḥ  Lank 
abhūtvā yasya cotpādo bhūtvā cāpi vinaśyati 
pratyayaiḥ sadasaccāpi na te me śāsane sthitāḥ  Lank 
anādyanidhanābhāvādbhūtalakṣaṇasaṃsthitāḥ 
kāraṇakaravalloke na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ  Lank 
atīto vidyate bhāvo vidyate ca anāgataḥ 
pratyakṣo vidyate yasmāttasmādbhāvā ajātakāḥ  Lank 
pariṇāmakālasaṃsthānaṃ bhūtabhāvendriyeṣu ca 
antarābhavasaṃgrāhaṃ ye kalpanti na te budhāḥ  Lank 
na pratītyasamutpannaṃ lokaṃ varṇanti vai jināḥ 
kiṃ tu pratyayamevāyaṃ loko gandharvasaṃnibhaḥ  Lank 
dharmasaṃketa evāyaṃ tasmiṃstadidamucyate 
saṃketācca pṛthagbhūto na jāto na nirudhyate  Lank 
darpaṇe udake netre bhāṇḍeṣu ca maṇīṣu ca 
bimbaṃ hi dṛśyate teṣu na ca bimbo 'sti kutracit  Lank 
bhāvābhāsaṃ tathā cittaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇā yathā nabhe 
dṛśyate citrarūpeṇa svapne vandhyauraso yathā  Lank 
na me yānaṃ mahāyānaṃ na ghoṣo na ca akṣarāḥ 
na satyā na vimokṣā vai na nirābhāsagocaram  Lank 
kiṃ tu yānaṃ mahāyānaṃ samādhivaśavartitā 
kāyaṃ manomayaṃ citraṃ vaśitāpuṣpamaṇḍitam  Lank 
Vaidya 
ekatvena pṛthaktvena bhāvo vai pratyaye na tu 
janma samāsamevoktaṃ nirodho nāśa eva hi  Lank 
ajātaśūnyatā caikamekaṃ jāteṣu śūnyatā 
ajātaśūnyatā śreṣṭhā naśyate jātaśūnyatā  Lank 
tathatā śūnyatā koṭī nirvāṇaṃ dharmadhātuvat 
kāyo manomayaṃ citraṃ paryāyairdeśitaṃ mayā  Lank 
sūtravinayābhidharmeṇa viśuddhiṃ kalpayanti ye 
granthato na tu arthena na te nairātmyamāśritāḥ  Lank 
na tīrthikairna buddhaiśca na mayā na ca kenacit 
pratyayaiḥ sādhitāstitvaṃ kathaṃ nāstirbhaviṣyati  Lank 
kena prasādhitāstitvaṃ pratyayairyasya nāstitā 
utpādavādadurdṛṣṭyā nāstyastīti vikalpayet  Lank 
yasya notpadyate kiṃcinna kiṃcittaṃ nirudhyate 
tasyāstināsti nopaiti viviktaṃ paśyato jagat  Lank 
dṛśyate śaśaviṣāṇākhyaṃ vikalpo vidyate nṛṇām 
ye tu kalpenti te bhrāntā mṛgatṛṣṇāṃ yathā mṛgāḥ  Lank 
vikalpābhiniveśena vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate 
nirhetukaṃ vikalpaṃ hi vikalpo 'pi na yujyate  Lank 
ajale ca jalagrāho mṛgatṛṣṇā yathā nabhe 
dṛśyate 'rtho hi bālānāmāryāṇāṃ na viśeṣataḥ  Lank 
āryāṇāṃ darśanaṃ śuddhaṃ vimokṣatrayasaṃbhavam 
utpādabhaṅganirmuktaṃ nirābhāsapracāriṇam  Lank 
gāmbhīryodāryavaipulyaṃ jñānaṃ kṣetrān vibhūti ca 
deśemi jinaputrāṇāṃ śrāvakāṇāmanityatām  Lank 
anityaṃ tribhavaṃ śūnyamātmātmīyavivarjitam 
śrāvakāṇāṃ ca deśemi tathā sāmānyalakṣaṇam  Lank 
sarvadharmeṣvasaṃsaktirvivekā hyekacārikā 
pratyekajinaputrāṇāṃ phalaṃ deśemyatarkikam  Lank 
svabhāvakalpitaṃ bāhyaṃ paratantraṃ ca dehinām 
apaśyannātmasaṃbhrāntiṃ tataścittaṃ pravartate  Lank 
Vaidya 
daśamī tu bhavetprathamī prathamī cāṣṭamī bhavet 
navamī saptamī cāpi saptamī cāṣṭamī bhavet  Lank 
dvitīyā tu tṛtīyā syāccaturthī pañcamī bhavet 
tṛtīyā tu bhavetṣaṣṭhī nirābhāse kramaḥ kutaḥ  Lank 
nirābhāso hi bhāvānāmabhāvo nāsti yoginām 
bhāvābhāvasamatvena āryāṇāṃ jāyate phalam  Lank 
kathaṃ hyabhāvo bhāvānāṃ kurute samatāṃ katham 
yadā cittaṃ na jānāti bāhyamadhyātmikaṃ calam 
tadā tu kurute nāśaṃ samatācittadarśanāt  Lank 
anādimati saṃsāre bhāvagrāhopagūhitam 
bālaiḥ kīla yathā kīlaṃ pralobhya vinivartate  Lank 
taddhetukaṃ tadālambyaṃ manogatisamāśrayam 
hetuṃ dadāti cittasya vijñānaṃ ca samāśritam  Lank 
vaipākikādadhiṣṭhānāṃ nikāyagatisaṃbhavāt 
labhyante yena vai svapne abhijñāśca caturvidhāḥ  Lank 
svapne ca labhyate yacca yacca buddhaprasādataḥ 
nikāyagatigotrā ye te vijñānavipākajāḥ  Lank 
vāsanairbhāvitaṃ cittaṃ bhāvābhāsaṃ pravartate 
bālā yadā na budhyante utpādaṃ deśayettadā  Lank 
yāvadvākyaṃ vikalpeti bhāvaṃ vai lakṣaṇānvitam 
tāvadvibudhyate cittamapaśyan hi svavibhramam  Lank 
utpādo varṇyate kasmātkasmāddṛśyaṃ na varṇyate 
adṛśyaṃ dṛśyamānaṃ hi kasya kiṃ varṇyate kutaḥ  Lank 
svacchaṃ cittaṃ svabhāvena manaḥ kaluṣakārakam 
manaśca sahavijñānairvāsanāṃ kṣipate sadā  Lank 
ālayo muñcate kāyaṃ manaḥ prārthayate gatim 
vijñānaṃ viṣayābhāsaṃ bhrāntiṃ dṛṣṭvā pralabhyate  Lank 
madīyaṃ dṛśyate cittaṃ bāhyamarthaṃ na vidyate 
evaṃ vibhāvayedbhrāntiṃ tathatāṃ cāpyanusmaret  Lank 
dhyāyināṃ viṣayaḥ karma buddhamāhātmyameva ca 
etāni trīṇyacintyāni acintyaṃ vijñānagocaram  Lank 
Vaidya 
anāgatamatītaṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ pudgalaṃ vacaḥ 
saṃvṛtyā deśayāmyetān paramārthastvanakṣaraḥ  Lank 
naikāyikāśca tīrthyāśca dṛṣṭimekāṃśamāśritāḥ 
cittamātre visaṃmūḍhā bhāvaṃ kalpenti bāhiram  Lank 
pratyekabodhiṃ buddhatvamarhattvaṃ buddhadarśanam 
gūḍhabījaṃ bhavedbodhau svapne vai sidhyate tu yaḥ  Lank 
kutra keṣāṃ kathaṃ kasmātkimarthaṃ ca vadāhi me 
mayācittamatiśāntaṃ sadasatpakṣadeśanām  Lank 
cittamātre vimūḍhānāṃ māyānāstyastideśanām 
utpādabhaṅgasaṃyuktaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam  Lank 
vikalpo mano nāma vijñānaiḥ pañcabhiḥ saha 
bimbaughajalatulyādau cittabījaṃ pravartate  Lank 
yadā cittaṃ manaścāpi vijñānaṃ na pravartate 
tadā manomayaṃ kāyaṃ labhate buddhabhūmi ca  Lank 
pratyayā dhātavaḥ skandhā dharmāṇāṃ ca svalakṣaṇam 
prajñaptiṃ pudgalaṃ cittaṃ svapnakeśoṇḍukopamāḥ  Lank 
māyāsvapnopamaṃ lokaṃ dṛṣṭvā tattvaṃ samāśrayet 
tattvaṃ hi lakṣaṇairmuktaṃ yuktihetuvivarjitam  Lank 
pratyātmavedyamāryāṇāṃ vihāraṃ tu smaretsadā 
yuktihetuvisaṃmūḍhaṃ lokaṃ tattve niveśayet  Lank 
sarvaprapañcopaśamādbhrānto nābhipravartate 
prajñā yāvadvikalpante bhrāntistāvatpravartate  Lank 
naiḥsvabhāvyaṃ ca bhāvaṃ ca śūnyā vai nityānityatā 
utpādavādināṃ dṛṣṭirna tvanutpādavādinām  Lank 
ekatvamanyatvobhayāmīśvarācca yadṛcchayā 
kālāpradhānādanyebhiḥ pratyayaiḥ kalpyate jagat  Lank 
saṃsārabījaṃ vijñānaṃ sati dṛśye pravartate 
kuḍye sati yathā citraṃ parijñānānnirudhyate  Lank 
māyāpuruṣavannṝṇāṃ mṛtajanma pravartate 
mohāttathaiva bālānāṃ bandhamokṣaṃ pravartate  Lank 
adhyātmabāhyaṃ dvividhaṃ dharmāśca pratyayāni ca 
etadvibhāvayan yogī nirābhāse pratiṣṭhate  Lank 
Vaidya 
na vāsanairbhidyate cittaṃ na cittaṃ vāsanaiḥ saha 
abhinnalakṣaṇaṃ cittaṃ vāsanaiḥ pariveṣṭitam  Lank 
malavadvāsanā yasya manovijñānasaṃbhavā 
paṭaśuklopamaṃ cittaṃ vāsanairna virājate  Lank 
yathā na bhāvo nābhāvo gaganaṃ kathyate mayā 
ālayaṃ hi tathā kāye bhāvābhāvavivarjitam  Lank 
manovijñānavyāvṛttaṃ cittaṃ kāluṣyavarjitam 
sarvadharmāvabodhena cittaṃ buddhaṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
trisaṃtativyavacchinnaṃ sattāsattāvivarjitam 
cātuṣkoṭikayā muktaṃ bhavaṃ māyopamaṃ sadā  Lank 
dve svabhāvo bhavetsapta bhūmayaścittasaṃbhavāḥ 
śeṣā bhaveyurniṣpannā bhūmayo buddhabhūmi ca  Lank 
rūpī cārūpyadhātuśca kāmadhātuśca nirvṛtiḥ 
asmin kalevare sarvaṃ kathitaṃ cittagocaram  Lank 
upalabhyate yadā yāvadbhrāntistāvatpravartate 
bhrāntiḥ svacittasaṃbodhānna pravartate na nivartate  Lank 
anutpāde kāraṇābhāvo bhāve saṃsārasaṃgrahaḥ 
māyādisadṛśaṃ paśyan lakṣaṇaṃ na vikalpayet  Lank 
triyānamekayānaṃ ca ayānaṃ ca vadāmyaham 
bālānāṃ mandabuddhīnāmāryāṇāṃ ca viviktatām  Lank 
utpattirdvividhā mahyaṃ lakṣaṇādhigamau ca yā 
caturvidho nayavidhiḥ siddhāntaṃ yuktideśanā  Lank 
saṃsthānākṛtiviśeṣairbhrāntiṃ dṛṣṭvā vikalpyate 
nāmasaṃsthānavirahātsvabhāvamāryagocaram  Lank 
vikalpena kalpyate yāvattāvatkalpitalakṣaṇam 
vikalpakalpanābhāvātsvabhāvamāryagocaram  Lank 
nityaṃ ca śāśvataṃ tattvaṃ gotraṃ vastusvabhāvakam 
tathatā cittanirmuktaṃ kalpanaiśca vivarjitam  Lank 
yadyadvastu na śuddhiḥ syātsaṃkleśo nāpi kasyacit 
yasmācca śuṃdhyate cittaṃ saṃkleśaścāpi dṛśyate 
tasmāttattvaṃ bhavedvastu viśuddhamāryagocaram  Lank 
Vaidya 
pratyayairjanitaṃ lokaṃ vikalpaiśca vivarjitam 
māyādisvapnasadṛśaṃ vipaśyanto vimucyate  Lank 
dauṣṭhulyavāsanāścitrāścittena saha saṃyutāḥ 
bahirdhā dṛśyate nṝṇāṃ na hi cittasya dharmatā  Lank 
cittasya dharmatā śuddhā na cittaṃ bhrāntisaṃbhavam 
bhrāntiśca dauṣṭhulyamayī tena cittaṃ na dṛśyate  Lank 
bhrāntimātraṃ bhavettattvaṃ tattvaṃ nānyatra vidyate 
na saṃskāre na cānyatra kiṃ tu saṃskāradarśanāt  Lank 
lakṣyalakṣaṇanirmuktaṃ yadā paśyati saṃskṛtam 
vidhūtaṃ hi bhavettena svacittaṃ paśyato jagat  Lank 
cittamātraṃ samāruhya bāhyamarthaṃ na kalpayet 
tathatālambane sthitvā cittamātramatikramet  Lank 
cittamātramatikramya nirābhāsamatikramet 
nirābhāsasthito yogī mahāyānaṃ sa paśyati  Lank 
anābhogagatiḥ śāntā praṇidhānairviśodhitā 
jñānamanātmakaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nirābhāse na paśyati  Lank 
cittasya gocaraṃ paśyetpaśyejjñānasya gocaram 
prajñāyā gocaraṃ paśyellakṣaṇe na pramuhyate  Lank 
cittasya duḥkhasatyaṃ samudayo jñānagocaraḥ 
dve satye buddhabhūmiśca prajñā yatra pravartate  Lank 
phalaprāptiśca nirvāṇaṃ mārgamaṣṭāṅgikaṃ tathā 
sarvadharmāvabodhena buddhajñānaṃ viśudhyate  Lank 
cakṣuśca rūpamāloka ākāśaśca manastathā 
ebhirutpadyate nṝṇāṃ vijñānaṃ hyālayodbhavam  Lank 
grāhyaṃ grāho grahītā ca nāsti nāma hyavastukam 
nirhetukaṃ vikalpaṃ ye manyanti hi na te budhāḥ  Lank 
arthe nāma hyasaṃbhūtamartho nāmni tathaiva ca 
hetvahetusamutpannaṃ vikalpaṃ na vikalpayet  Lank 
sarvabhāvasvabhāvo 'san vacanaṃ hi tathāpyasat 
śūnyatāṃ śūnyatārthaṃ vā bālo 'paśyan vidhāvati  Lank 
Vaidya 
satyasthitiṃ manyanayā dṛṣṭvā prajñaptideśanā 
ekatvaṃ pañcadhāsiddhamidaṃ satyaṃ prahīyate  Lank 
prapañcamārabhedyaśca astināsti vyatikramet 
nāsticchando bhave mithyāsaṃjñā nairātmyadarśanāt  Lank 
śāśvataṃ hi sakartṛtvaṃ vādamātrapravartitam 
satyaṃ paraṃ hyavaktavyaṃ nirodhe dharmadarśanam  Lank 
ālayaṃ hi samāśritya mano vai saṃpravartate 
cittaṃ manaśca saṃśritya vijñānaṃ saṃpravartate  Lank 
samāropaṃ samāropya tathatā cittadharmatā 
etadvibhāvayan yogī cittamātrajñatāṃ labhet  Lank 
manaśca lakṣaṇaṃ vastu nityānitye na manyate 
utpādaṃ cāpyanutpādaṃ yogī yoge na manyate  Lank 
arthadvayaṃ na kalpenti vijñānaṃ hyālayodbhavam 
ekamarthaṃ dvicittena na jānīte tadudbhavam  Lank 
na vaktā na ca vācyo 'sti na śūnyaṃ cittadarśanāt 
adarśanātsvacittasya dṛṣṭijālaṃ pravartate  Lank 
pratyayāgamanaṃ nāsti indriyāṇi na kecana 
na dhātavo na ca skandhā na rāgo na ca saṃskṛtam  Lank 
karmaṇo 'gniṃ na vai pūrvaṃ na kṛtaṃ na ca saṃskṛtam 
na koṭi na ca vai śaktirna mokṣo na ca bandhanam  Lank 
avyākṛto na bhāvo 'sti dharmādharmaṃ na caiva hi 
na kālaṃ na ca nirvāṇaṃ dharmatāpi na vidyate  Lank 
na ca buddho na satyāni na phalaṃ na ca hetavaḥ 
viparyayo na nirvāṇaṃ vibhavo nāsti saṃbhavaḥ  Lank 
dvādaśāṅgaṃ na caivāsti antānantaṃ na caiva hi 
sarvadṛṣṭiprahāṇāya cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
kleśāḥ karmapathā dehaḥ kartāraśca phalaṃ ca vai 
marīcisvapnasaṃkāśā gandharvanagaropamāḥ  Lank 
cittamātravyavasthānādvayāvṛttaṃ bhāvalakṣaṇam 
cittamātrapratiṣṭhānācchāśvatocchedadarśanam  Lank 
Vaidya 
skandhā na santi nirvāṇe na caivātmā na lakṣaṇam 
cittamātrāvatāreṇa mokṣagrāhānnivartate  Lank 
bhūdṛśyahetuko doṣo bahirdhā khyāyate nṛṇām 
cittaṃ hyadṛśyasaṃbhūtaṃ tena cittaṃ na dṛśyate  Lank 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhānā khyāyate vāsanā nṛṇām 
cittaṃ na bhāvo nābhāvo vāsane na virājate  Lank 
malo vai khyāyate śukle na śukle khyāyate malaḥ 
ghane hi gaganaṃ yadvattathā cittaṃ na dṛśyate  Lank 
cittena cīyate karma jñānena ca vicīyate 
prajñayā ca nirābhāsaṃ prabhāvaṃ cādhigacchati  Lank 
cittaṃ viṣayasaṃbaddhaṃ jñānaṃ tarke pravartate 
nirābhāse viśeṣe ca jñānaṃ vai saṃpravartate  Lank 
cittaṃ manaśca vijñānaṃ saṃjñā vai kalpavarjitā 
avikalpadharmatāṃ prāptāḥ śrāvakā na jinātmajāḥ  Lank 
kṣānte kṣānte viśeṣe vai jñānaṃ tāthāgataṃ śubham 
saṃjāyate viśeṣārthaṃ samudācāravarjitam  Lank 
parikalpitasvabhāvo 'sti paratantro na vidyate 
kalpitaṃ gṛhyate bhrāntyā paratantraṃ na kalpyate  Lank 
cittaṃ hyabhūtasaṃbhūtaṃ na cittaṃ dṛśyate kvacit 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhānaṃ khyāyate vāsanā nṛṇām  Lank 
na sarvabhautikaṃ rūpamasti rūpamabhautikam 
gandharvasvapnamāyā yā mṛgatṛṣṇā hyabhautikā  Lank 
prajñā hi trividhā mahyamāryaṃ yena prabhāvitam 
cittaṃ hyadṛśyasaṃbhūtaṃ tena cittaṃ na dṛśyate  Lank 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhānā khyāyate vāsanā nṛṇām 
lakṣaṇaṃ kalpate yena yaḥ svabhāvān vṛṇoti ca  Lank 
yānadvayavisaṃyuktā prajñā hyābhāsavarjitā 
saṃbhavābhiniveśena śrāvakāṇāṃ pravartate 
cittamātrāvatāreṇa prajñā tāthāgatī 'malā  Lank 
sato hi asataścāpi pratyayairyadi jāyate 
ekatvānyatvadṛṣṭiśca avaśyaṃ taiḥ samāśritā  Lank 
Vaidya 
vividhāgatirhi nirvṛttā yathā māyā na sidhyati 
nimittaṃ hi tathā citraṃ kalpyamānaṃ na sidhyati  Lank 
nimittadauṣṭhulyamayaṃ bandhanaṃ cittasaṃbhavam 
parikalpitaṃ hyajānānaiḥ paratantraṃ vikalpyate  Lank 
ya eva kalpito bhāvaḥ paratantraṃ tadeva hi 
kalpitaṃ hi vicitrābhaṃ paratantraṃ vikalpyate  Lank 
saṃvṛtiḥ paramārthaśca tṛtīyaṃ nāsti hetukam 
kalpitaṃ saṃvṛtirhyuktā tacchedādāryagocaraḥ  Lank 
yathā hi yogināṃ vastu citramekaṃ virājate 
na hyasti citratā tatra tathā kalpitalakṣaṇam  Lank 
yathā hi taimiraiścitraṃ kalpyate rūpadarśanam 
timiraṃ na rūpaṃ nārūpaṃ paratantraṃ tathā budhaiḥ  Lank 
hemaṃ syāttu yathā śuddhaṃ jalaṃ kaluṣavarjitam 
gaganaṃ hi ghanābhāvāttathā śuddhaṃ vikalpitam  Lank 
śrāvakastrividho mahyaṃ nirmitaḥ praṇidhānajaḥ 
rāgadveṣavisaṃyuktaḥ śrāvako dharmasaṃbhavaḥ  Lank 
bodhisattvo 'pi trividho buddhānāṃ nāsti lakṣaṇam 
citte citte tu sattvānāṃ buddhabimbaṃ vidṛśyate  Lank 
nāsti vai kalpito bhāvaḥ paratantraṃ ca vidyate 
samāropāpavādaṃ ca vikalpaṃ no vinaśyati  Lank 
kalpitaṃ yadyabhāvaḥ syātparatantrasvabhāvataḥ 
vinābhāvena vai bhāvaṃ bhāvaścābhāvasaṃbhavaḥ  Lank 
parikalpitaṃ samāśritya paratantraṃ pralabhyate 
nimittanāmasaṃbandhājjāyate parikalpitam  Lank 
atyantaṃ cāpyaniṣpannaṃ kalpitena parodbhavam 
tadā prajñāyate śuddhaḥ svabhāavaḥ pāramārthikaḥ  Lank 
parikalpitaṃ daśavidhaṃ paratantraṃ ca ṣaḍvidham 
tathatā ca pratyātmagatimato nāsti viśeṣaṇam  Lank 
pañca dharmā bhavettatvaṃ svabhāvā hi trayastathā 
etadvibhāvayan yogī tathatāṃ nātivartate  Lank 
nakṣatrameghasaṃsthānaṃ somabhāskarasaṃnibham 
cittaṃ saṃdṛśyate nṝṇāṃ dṛśyābhaṃ vāsanoditam  Lank 
Vaidya 
bhūtālabdhātmakā hyete na lakṣyaṃ na ca lakṣaṇam 
sarve bhūtamayā bhūtā yadi rūpaṃ hi bhautikam  Lank 
asaṃbhūtā mahābhūtā nāsti bhūteṣu bhautikam 
kāraṇaṃ hi mahābhūtāḥ kāryaṃ bhūsalilādayaḥ  Lank 
dravyaprajñaptirūpaṃ ca māyājātikṛtaṃ tathā 
svapnagandharvarūpaṃ ca mṛgatṛṣṇā ca pañcamam  Lank 
icchantikaṃ pañcavidhaṃ gotrāḥ pañca tathā bhavet

skandhabhedāścaturviśadrūpaṃ cāṣṭavidhaṃ bhavet

vimuktayastathā tisraścittadhārā caturvidhā

kāraṇaiśca visaṃyuktaṃ dṛṣṭidoṣavivarjitam 
pratyātmavedyamacalaṃ mahāyānamanuttaram  Lank 
utpādaṃ cāpyanutpādamaṣṭadhā navadhā bhavet 
ekānupūrvasamayaṃ siddhāntamekameva ca  Lank 
ārūpyadhātvaṣṭavidhaṃ dhyānabhedaśca ṣaḍvidhaḥ 
pratyekajinaputrāṇāṃ niryāṇaṃ saptadhā bhavet  Lank 
adhvatrayaṃ na caivāsti nityānityaṃ ca nāsti vai 
kriyā karma phalaṃ caiva svapnakāryaṃ tathā bhavet  Lank 
antādyāsaṃbhavā buddhāḥ śrāvakāśca jinaurasāḥ 
cittaṃ dṛśyavisaṃyuktaṃ māyādharmopamaṃ sadā  Lank 
garbhaścakraṃ tathā jātirnaiṣkramyaṃ tuṣitālayam 
sarvakṣetragatāścāpi dṛśyante na ca yonijāḥ  Lank 
saṃkrāntiṃ saṃcaraṃ sattvaṃ deśanā nirvṛtistathā

dhyānaṃ yānālayaprāptiracintyaphalagocaram  Lank 
candranakṣatragotrāṇi nṛpagotrā surālayam 
yakṣagandharvagotrāṇi karmajā tṛṣṇasaṃbhavā  Lank 
Vaidya 
acintyapariṇāmī ca cyutirvāsanasaṃyutā

rājāno rājaputrāśca amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinastathā 
piṇḍārthe nopadeśeta yogī yogaparāyaṇaḥ  Lank

vihāre yatra vai dhūmaḥ pacyate vidhivatsadā 
uddiśya yatkṛtaṃ cāpi na tatkalpati yoginām  Lank 
Vaidya 
utpādabhaṅganirmuktaṃ sadasatpakṣavarjitam

svakalpakalpitaṃ lokaṃ citraṃ vai vāsanoditam 
pratipaśyetsadā yogī māyāsvapnopamaṃ bhavam  Lank 
apavādasamāropavarjitaṃ darśanaṃ sadā 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ tribhavaṃ na vikalpayet  Lank

vinayātsūtrayuktibhyāṃ tattvaṃ saṃhṛtya yogavit

Vaidya 
cittamātrāvabodhena bāhyabhāvā vyudāśrayā 
vinivṛttirvikalpasya pratipat saiva madhyamā  Lank 
cittamātraṃ na dṛśyanti dṛśyābhāvānna jāyate 
pratipanmadhyamā caiṣā mayā cānyaiśca deśitā  Lank 
utpādaṃ cāpyanutpādaṃ bhāvābhāvaśca śūnyatā

vikalpavṛttyā bhāvo na mokṣaṃ kalpenti bāliśāḥ 
na cittavṛttyasaṃbodhāddvayagrāhaḥ prahīyate  Lank 
svacittadṛśyasaṃbodhāddvayagrāhaḥ prahīyate

asyāvabodhādbuddhatvaṃ mayā buddhaiśca deśitam

vicitrarūpasaṃsthānāścittamātre gatiṃgatāḥ  Lank

Vaidya 
nimittaṃ paratantraṃ hi yannāma tatra kalpitam 
parikalpitanimittaṃ pāratantryātpravartate  Lank

niṣpanno nāsti vai bhāvaḥ kathaṃ buddhyā prakalpyate  Lank

ṣaṭtriṃśadbuddhabhedāśca daśa bhedāḥ pṛthakpṛthak

Vaidya 
cittaṃ manaśca vijñānaṃ lakṣaṇārthaṃ prakalpyate

udadheśca taraṃgāṇāṃ yathā nāsti viśeṣaṇam 
vijñānānāṃ tathā citte pariṇāmo na labhyate  Lank 
cittena cīyate karma manasā ca vicīyate

nīlaraktaprakāra hi vijñānaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām

Vaidya 
deśanāvyabhicārī ca tattvaṃ hyakṣaravarjitam

Vaidya 
cittalakṣaṇanirmuktaṃ vijñānamanavarjitam

Vaidya 
deśanādharmaniṣyando yacca niṣyandanirmitam 
buddhā hyete bhavetpaurāḥ śeṣā nirmāṇavigrahāḥ  Lank 
dṛśyaṃ na vidyate cittaṃ cittaṃ dṛśyātpramuhyate

tārkikāṇāmaviṣayaṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ na caiva hi

astitvasādhakā nāsti asti nāstitvasādhakam  Lank 
aṇuśo vibhajya dravyaṃ na vai rūpaṃ vikalpayet 
cittamātravyavasthānaṃ kudṛṣṭyā na prasīdati  Lank 
mā śūnyatāṃ vikalpetha māśūnyamiti vā punaḥ 
nāstyasti kalpanaiveyaṃ kalpyamarthaṃ na vidyate  Lank 
guṇāṇudravyasaṃghātai rūpaṃ bālairvikalpyate 
ekaikamaṇuśo nāsti ato 'pyarthaṃ na vidyate  Lank 
svacittaṃ dṛśyasaṃsthānaṃ bahirdhā khyāyate nṛṇām 
bāhyaṃ na vidyate dṛśyamato 'pyarthaṃ na vidyate  Lank 
citraṃ keśoṇḍukaṃ māyāṃ svapna gandharvameva ca 
alātaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇā ca asantaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām  Lank 
nityānityaṃ tathaikatvamubhayaṃ nobhayaṃ tathā 
anādidoṣasaṃbaddhā bālāḥ kalpenti mohitāḥ  Lank 
yānavyavasthā naivāsti yānamekaṃ vadāmyaham 
parikarṣaṇārthaṃ bālānāṃ yānabhedaṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
vimuktayastathā tisro dharmanairātmyameva ca 
samatājñānakleśākhyā vimuktyā te vivarjitāḥ  Lank 
yathā hi kāṣṭhamudadhau taraṃgairvipravāhyate 
tathā ca śrāvako mūḍho lakṣaṇena pravāhyate  Lank 
niṣṭhāgatirna tattasyā na ca bhūyo nivartate 
samādhikāyaṃ saṃprāpya ā kalpānna prabudhyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
vāsanākleśasaṃbaddhā paryutthānairvisaṃyutāḥ 
samādhimadamattāste dhātau tiṣṭhantyanāsrave  Lank 
yathā hi mattaḥ puruṣo madyābhāvādvibudhyate 
tathā te buddhadharmākhyaṃ kāyaṃ prāpsyanti māmakam  Lank 
paṅkamagno yathā hastī itastato na dhāvati 
samādhimadamagnā vai tathā tiṣṭhanti śrāvakāḥ  Lank 
adhiṣṭhānaṃ narendrāṇāṃ praṇīdhānairviśodhitam 
abhiṣekasamādhyādyaṃ prathamā daśamī ca vai  Lank 
ākāśaṃ śaśaśṛṅgaṃ ca vandhyāyāḥ putra eva ca 
asantaścābhilapyante tathā bhāveṣu kalpanā  Lank 
vāsanāhetukaṃ lokaṃ nāsanna sadasatkvacit 
ye paśyanti vimucyante dharmanairātmyakovidāḥ  Lank 
svabhāvakalpitaṃ nāma parabhāvaśca tantrajaḥ 
niṣpannaṃ tathatetyuktaṃ sūtre sūtre sadā mayā  Lank 
vyañjanaṃ padakāyaṃ ca nāma cāpi viśeṣataḥ 
bālāḥ sajanti durmedhā yathā paṅke mahāgajāḥ  Lank 
devayānaṃ brahmayānaṃ śrāvakīyaṃ tathaiva ca 
tāthāgataṃ ca pratyekaṃ yānānyetān vadāmyaham  Lank 
yānānāṃ nāsti vai niṣṭhā yāvaccittaṃ pravartate 
citte tu vai parāvṛtte na yānaṃ na ca yāyinaḥ  Lank 
cittaṃ vikalpo vijñaptirmano vijñānameva ca 
ālayaṃ tribhavaśceṣṭā ete cittasya paryayāḥ  Lank 
āyuruṣmātha vijñānamālayo jīvitendriyam 
manaśca manavijñānaṃ vikalpasya viśeṣaṇam  Lank 
cittena dhāryate kāyo mano manyati vai sadā 
vijñānaṃ cittaviṣayaṃ vijñānaiḥ saha chindati  Lank 
tṛṣṇā hi mātā ityuktā avidyā ca tathā pitā 
viṣayāvabodhādvijñānaṃ buddha ityupadiśyate  Lank 
arhanto hyanuśayāḥ skandhāḥ saṃghaḥ skandhakapañcakaḥ 
nirantarāntaracchedātkarma hyānantaraṃ bhavet  Lank 
Vaidya 
nairātmyasya dvayaṃ kleśāstathaivāvaraṇadvayam 
acintyapariṇāminyāścyuterlābhāstathāgatāḥ  Lank 
siddhāntaśca nayaścāpi pratyātmaṃ śāsanaṃ ca vai 
ye paśyanti vibhāgajñā na te tarkavaśaṃ gatāḥ  Lank 
na bhāvo vidyate satyaṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate 
abhāvena tu vai mokṣaṃ kathaṃ necchanti tārkikāḥ  Lank 
utpādabhaṅgasaṃbaddhaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ pratipaśyataḥ 
dṛṣṭidvayaṃ prapuṣṇanti na ca jānanti pratyayān  Lank 
ekameva bhavetsatyaṃ nirvāṇaṃ manavarjitam 
kadalīsvapnamāyābhaṃ lokaṃ paśyedvikalpitam  Lank 
rāgo na vidyate dveṣo mohaścāpi na pudgalaḥ 
tṛṣṇāyā hyuditāḥ skandhā vidyante svapnasādṛśāḥ  Lank 
yasyāṃ ca rātryāṃ dhigamo yasyāṃ ca parinirvṛtaḥ 
etasminnantare nāsti mayā kiṃcitprakāśitam  Lank 
pratyātmadharmasthititāṃ saṃdhāya kathitaṃ mayā 
taiśca buddhairmayā caiva na ca kiṃcidviśeṣitam  Lank 
dravyavadvidyate hyātmā skandhā lakṣaṇavarjitāḥ 
skandhā vidyanti bhāvena ātmā teṣu na vidyate  Lank 
pratipattiṃ vibhāvanto kleśairmānuṣasaṃgamaiḥ 
mucyate sarvaduḥkhebhyaḥ svacittaṃ paśyato jagat  Lank 
kāraṇaiḥ pratyayaiścāpi yeṣāṃ lokaḥ pravartate 
cātuṣkoṭikayā yukto na te mannayakovidāḥ  Lank 
sadasanna jāyate loko nāsanna sadasatkvacit 
pratyayaiḥ kāraṇaiścāpi kathaṃ bālairvikalpyate  Lank 
na sannāsanna sadasadyadā lokaṃ prapaśyati 
tadā vyāvartate cittaṃ nairātmyaṃ cādhigacchati  Lank 
anutpannāḥ sarvabhāvā yasmātpratyayasaṃbhavāḥ 
kāryaṃ hi pratyayāḥ sarve na kāryājjāyate bhavaḥ  Lank 
kāryaṃ na jāyate kāryaṃ dvitvaṃ kārye prasajyate 
na ca dvitvaprasaṅgena kāryābhāvopalabhyate  Lank 
ālambālambavigataṃ yadā paśyati saṃskṛtam 
nimittaṃ cittamātraṃ hi cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
Vaidya 
mātrāsvabhāvasaṃsthānaṃ pratyayairbhāvavarjitam 
niṣṭhābhāvaparaṃ brahma etāṃ mātrāṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
prajñaptisatyato hyātmā dravyaḥ sa hi na vidyate 
skandhānāṃ skandhatā tadvatprajñaptyā na tu dravyataḥ  Lank 
caturvidhā vai samatā lakṣaṇaṃ hetubhājanam 
nairātmyasamatā caiva caturthā yogayoginām  Lank 
vyāvṛttiḥ sarvadṛṣṭīnāṃ kalpyakalpanavarjitā 
anupalambho hyajātiśca cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
na bhāvaṃ nāpi cābhāvaṃ bhāvābhāvavivarjitam 
tathatā cittanirmuktaṃ cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
tathatā śūnyatā koṭī nirvāṇaṃ dharmadhātukam 
kāyaṃ manomayaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
vikalpavāsanābaddhaṃ vicitraṃ cittasaṃbhavam 
bahirdhā jāyate nṝṇāṃ cittamātraṃ hi laukikam  Lank 
dṛśyaṃ na vidyate bāhyaṃ cittacitraṃ vidṛśyate 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
śrāvakāṇāṃ kṣayajñānaṃ buddhānāṃ janmasaṃbhavam 
pratyekajinaputrāṇāṃ asaṃkleśātpravartate  Lank 
bahirdhā nāsti vai rūpaṃ svacittaṃ dṛśyate bahiḥ 
anavabodhātsvacittasya bālāḥ kalpenti saṃskṛtam  Lank 
bāhyamarthamajānānaiḥ svacittacitradarśanam 
hetubhirvāryate mūḍhaiścātuṣkoṭikayojitaiḥ  Lank 
na hetavo na koṭyo vai dṛṣṭāntāvayavāni ca 
svacittaṃ hyarthasaṃkrāntaṃ yadi jānanti paṇḍitāḥ  Lank 
vikalpairna vikalpeta yadvikalpitalakṣaṇam 
kalpitaṃ ca samāśritya vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  Lank 
anyonyābhinnasaṃbandhādekavāsanahetukāḥ 
āgantukatvāttaddvayorna cittaṃ jāyate nṛṇām  Lank 
vikalpaṃ cittacaittārthī tribhave ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
yadarthābhāḥ pravartante svabhāvakalpito hi saḥ  Lank 
ābhāsabījasaṃyogāddvādaśāyatanāni vai 
āśrayālambyasaṃyogātprakriyā varṇyate mayā  Lank 
Vaidya 
yathā hi darpaṇe bimbaṃ keśoṇḍustimirasya vā 
tathā hi vāsanaiśchannaṃ cittaṃ paśyanti bāliśāḥ  Lank 
svavikalpakalpite hyarthe vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate 
artho na vidyate bāhyo yathā tīrthyairvikalpyate  Lank 
rajjuṃ yathā hyajānānāḥ sarpaṃ gṛhṇanti bāliśāḥ 
svacittārthamajānānā hyarthaṃ kalpenti bāhiram  Lank 
tathā hi rajjuṃ rajjutve ekatvānyatvavarjitam 
kiṃ tu svacittadoṣo 'yaṃ yena rajjurvikalpyate  Lank 
na hi yo yena bhāvena kalpyamāno na lakṣyate 
na tannāstyavagantavyaṃ dharmāṇāmeṣa dharmatā  Lank 
astitvapūrvakaṃ nāsti asti nāstitvapūrvakam 
ato nāsti na gantavyaṃ astitvaṃ na ca kalpayet  Lank 
kalpitaṃ kalpyamānaṃ hi yadidaṃ na tadātmakam 
anātmakaṃ kathaṃ dṛṣṭvā vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  Lank 
rūpaṃ rūpātmanā nāsti tathā ghaṭapaṭādayaḥ 
avidyamāne dṛśye tu vikalpastena jāyate  Lank 
vikalpaste yadi bhrāntāvanādimati saṃskṛte 
bhāvānāṃ bhāvatā kena bhrāmitā brūhi me mune  Lank 
bhāvānāṃ bhāvatā nāsti cittamātraṃ ca dṛśyate 
apaśyamānaḥ svacittaṃ vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  Lank 
kalpitaṃ yadi vai nāsti yathā kalpati bāliśaḥ 
anyathā vidyate cāsau na ca buddhyāvagamyate  Lank 
āryāṇāṃ yadi vā so 'sti nāsau bālairvikalpitaḥ 
āryāṇāmatha mithyāsau āryā bālaiḥ samaṃ gatāḥ  Lank 
āryāṇāṃ nāsti vai bhrāntiryasmāccittaṃ viśodhitam 
aśuddhacittasaṃtānā bālāḥ kalpenti kalpitam  Lank 
mātā yathā hi putrasya ākāśātphalamānayet 
etaddhi putra mā kranda gṛhṇa citramidaṃ phalam  Lank 
tathāhaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ vicitraiḥ kalpitaiḥ phalaiḥ 
pralobhya deśemi nayaṃ sadasatpakṣavarjitam  Lank 
abhūtvā yasya vai bhāvaḥ pratyayairna ca saṃkulaḥ 
ajātapūrvaṃ tajjātamalabdhātmakameva ca  Lank 
Vaidya 
alabdhātmakaṃ hyajātaṃ ca pratyayairna vinā kvacit 
utpannamapi te bhāvo pratyayairna vinā kvacit  Lank 
evaṃ samāsataḥ paśyan nāsanna sadasatkvacit 
pratyayairjāyate bhūtamavikalpyaṃ hi paṇḍitaiḥ  Lank 
ekatvānyatvakathāḥ kutīrthyāḥ kurvanti bāliśāḥ 
pratyayairna ca jānanti māyāsvapnopamaṃ jagat  Lank 
abhidhānaviṣayaṃ yānaṃ mahāyānamanuttaram 
arthaṃ sunītaṃ hi mayā na ca budhyanti bāliśāḥ  Lank 
mātsaryairye praṇītāni śrāvakaistīrthakaistathā 
vyabhicaranti te hyarthaṃ yasmāttarkeṇa deśitāḥ  Lank 
lakṣaṇaṃ bhāva saṃsthānaṃ nāma caiva caturvidham 
etadālambanīkṛtya kalpanā saṃpravartate  Lank 
ekadhā bahudhā ye tu brahmakāyavaśaṃgatāḥ 
somabhāskarayorbhāvā ye nāśenti na te sutāḥ  Lank 
āryadarśanasaṃpannā yathābhūtagatiṃgatāḥ 
saṃjñāvivartakuśalā vijñāne ca paraṃgatāḥ  Lank 
eṣā hi mudrā muktānāṃ putrāṇāṃ mama śāsane 
bhāvābhāvavinirmuktā gatyāgativivarjitā  Lank 
vyāvṛtte rūpavijñāne yadi karma vinaśyati 
nityānityaṃ na prāpnoti saṃsāraśca na vidyate  Lank 
vinirvṛttikāle pradhvastaṃ rūpaṃ deśānnivartate 
nāstyastidoṣanirmuktaṃ karma tiṣṭhati ālaye  Lank 
pradhvaṃsi patitaṃ rūpaṃ vijñānaṃ ca bhavālaye 
rūpavijñānasaṃbaddhaṃ na ca karma vinaśyati  Lank 
atha taiḥ saha saṃbaddhaṃ karma vai dhvasyate nṛṇām 
dhvaste tu karmasaṃbandhe na saṃsṛtirna nirvṛtiḥ  Lank 
atha dhvastamapi taiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃsāre yadi jāyate 
rūpaṃ ca tena saṃbaddhamabhinnatvādbhaviṣyati  Lank 
nābhinnaṃ na ca vai bhinnaṃ cittaṃ rūpaṃ vikalpanāt 
pradhvaṃso nāsti bhāvānāṃ sadasatpakṣavarjanāt  Lank 
Vaidya 
kalpitaḥ paratantraśca anyonyābhinnalakṣaṇāt 
rūpe hyanityatā yadvadanyonyajanakāśca vai  Lank 
anyo 'nanyavinirmuktaṃḥ kalpito nāvadhāryate 
nāstyasti kathaṃ bhavati rūpe cānityatā yathā  Lank 
kalpitena sudṛṣṭena paratantro na jāyate 
paratantreṇa dṛṣṭena kalpitastathatā bhavet  Lank 
kalpitaṃ hi vināśete mama netrī vinaśyate 
samāropāpavādaṃ ca kurvate mama śāsane  Lank 
evaṃvidhā yadā yasmin kāle syurdharmadūṣakāḥ 
sarve ca te hyasaṃkathyā mama netrīvināśakāḥ  Lank 
anālapyāśca vidvadbhirbhikṣukāryaṃ ca varjayet 
kalpitaṃ yatra nāśenti samāropāpavādinaḥ  Lank 
keśoṇḍukamāyābhaṃ svapnagandharvasādṛśam 
marīcyābhadṛśakalpo yeṣāṃ nāstyastidarśanāt  Lank 
nāsau śikṣati buddhānāṃ yasteṣāṃ saṃgrahe caret 
dvayāntapatitā hyete anyeṣāṃ ca vināśakāḥ  Lank 
viviktaṃ kalpitaṃ bhāvaṃ ye tu paśyanti yoginaḥ 
bhāvābhāvavinirmuktaṃ teṣāṃ vai saṃgrahe caret  Lank 
ākarā hi yathā loke suvarṇamaṇimuktijāḥ 
akarmahetukāścitrā upajīvyāśca bāliśām  Lank 
tathā hi sattvagotrāṇi citrā vai karmavarjitā 
dṛśyābhāvānna karmāsti na ca vai karmajā gatiḥ  Lank 
bhāvānāṃ bhāvatā nāsti yathā tvāryairvibhāvyate 
kiṃ tu vidyanti vai bhāvā yathā bālairvikalpitāḥ  Lank 
yadi bhāvā va vidyante yathā bālairvikalpitāḥ 
asatsu sattvabhāveṣu saṃkleśo nāsti kasyacit  Lank 
bhāvavaicitryasaṃkleśātsaṃsāraṃ indriyopagaḥ 
ajñānatṛṣṇāsaṃbaddhaḥ pravartate śarīriṇām  Lank 
yeṣāṃ tu bhāvo vai nāsti yathā bālairvikalpitaḥ 
teṣāṃ na vidyate vṛttirindriyāṇāṃ na yoginaḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
yadi bhāvā na vidyante bhāvasaṃsārahetavaḥ 
ayaṃ tena bhavenmokṣo bālānāṃ kriyavarjitaḥ  Lank 
bālāryāṇāṃ viśeṣaste bhāvābhāvātkathaṃ bhavet 
āryāṇāṃ nāsti vai bhāvo vimokṣatrayacāriṇām  Lank 
skandhāśca pudgalā dharmāḥ svasāmānyā alakṣaṇāḥ 
pratyayānīndriyāścaiva śrāvakāṇāṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
ahetucittamātraṃ tu vibhūti bhūmayastathā 
pratyātmatathatāṃ śuddhāṃ deśayāmi jinaurasām  Lank 
bhaviṣyantyanāgate kāle mama śāsanadūṣakāḥ 
kāṣāyavāsovasanāḥ sadasatkāryavādinaḥ  Lank 
asantaḥ pratyayairbhāvā vidyante hyāryagocaram 
kalpito nāsti vai bhāvaḥ kalpayiṣyanti tārkikāḥ  Lank 
bhaviṣyantyanāgate kāle kaṇabhugbālajātikāḥ 
asatkāryavādadurdṛṣṭyā janatāṃ nāśayanti ca  Lank 
aṇubhyo jagadutpannamaṇavaścāpyahetukāḥ 
nava dravyāṇi nityāni kudṛṣṭyā deśayiṣyati  Lank 
dravyairārabhyate dravyaṃ guṇaiścaiva guṇāstathā 
bhāvānāṃ bhāvatāmanyāṃ satīṃ vai nāśayiṣyati  Lank 
ādimān hi bhavelloko yadyabhūtvā pravartate 
pūrvā ca koṭirnaivāsti saṃsārasya vadāmyaham  Lank 
tribhavaḥ sarvasaṃkhyātaṃ yadyabhūtvā pravartate 
śvānoṣṭrakharaśṛṅgāṇāmutpattiḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ  Lank 
yadyabhūtvā bhaveccakṣū rūpaṃ vijñānameva ca 
kaṭamukuṭapaṭādyānāṃ mṛtpiṇḍātsaṃbhavo bhavet  Lank 
paṭaiśca vai kaṭo nāsti paṭo vai vīraṇaistathā 
eka ekatrā saṃbhūtaḥ pratyayaiḥ kiṃ na jāyate  Lank 
tajjīvaṃ taccharīraṃ ca yaccābhūtvā pravartate 
paravādā hyamī sarve mayā ca samudāhṛtāḥ  Lank 
uccārya pūrvapakṣaṃ ca matisteṣāṃ nivāryate 
nivārya tu matisteṣāṃ svapakṣaṃ deśayāmyaham  Lank 
atorthaṃ tīrthavādānāṃ kṛtamuccāraṇaṃ mayā 
mā me śiṣyagaṇo mūḍhaḥ sadasatpakṣamāśrayet  Lank 
Vaidya 
pradhānājjagadutpannaṃ kapilāṅgo 'pi durmatiḥ 
śiṣyebhyaḥ saṃprakāśeti guṇānāṃ ca vikāritā  Lank 
na bhūtaṃ nāpi cābhūtaṃ pratyayairna ca pratyayāḥ 
pratyayānāmasadbhāvādabhūtaṃ na pravartate  Lank 
sadasatpakṣavigato hetupratyayavarjitaḥ 
utpādabhaṅgarahitaḥ svapakṣo lakṣyavarjitaḥ  Lank 
māyāsvapnopamaṃ lokaṃ hetupratyayavarjitam 
ahetukaṃ sadā paśyan vikalpo na pravartate  Lank 
gandharvamṛgatṛṣṇābhaṃ keśoṇḍukanibhaṃ sadā 
sadasatpakṣavigataṃ hetupratyayavarjitam 
ahetukaṃ bhavaṃ paśyaṃścittadhārā viśudhyate  Lank 
vastu na vidyate paśyaṃścittamātraṃ na vidyate 
avastukaṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate  Lank 
vastumālambanīkṛtya cittaṃ saṃjāyate nṛṇām 
ahetukaṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate  Lank 
tathatā cittamātraṃ ca āryavastunayasya tu 
vidyante na ca vidyante na te mannayakovidāḥ  Lank 
grāhyagrāhakabhāvena yadi cittaṃ pravartate 
etaddhi laukikaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate  Lank 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ svapnavajjāyate yadi 
dvicittatā prasajyeta na ca cittaṃ dvilakṣaṇam  Lank 
svadhāraṃ hi yathā khaḍgaṃ svāgraṃ vai aṅguliryathā 
na chindate na spṛśate tathā cittaṃ svadarśane  Lank 
na paraṃ na ca vai tantraṃ kalpitaṃ vastumeva ca 
pañca dharmā dvicittaṃ ca nirābhāse na santi vai  Lank 
utpādakaṃ ca utpādyaṃ dvividhaṃ bhāvalakṣaṇam 
utpādakaṃ hi saṃdhāya naiḥsvabhāvyaṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
atha vaicitryasaṃsthāne kalpā ca yadi jāyate 
ākāśe śaśaśṛṅge ca arthābhāsaṃ bhaviṣyati  Lank 
arthābhāsaṃ bhaveccittaṃ tadarthaḥ syādakalpitaḥ 
na ca vai kalpito hyarthaścittādanyo 'bhilapyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
anādimati saṃsāre artho vai nāsti kutracit 
apuṣṭaṃ hi kathaṃ cittamarthābhāsaṃ pravartate  Lank 
yadyabhāvena puṣṭiḥ syācchaśaśṛṅge 'pi tadbhavet 
na cābhāvena vai puṣṭo vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  Lank 
yathāpi dānīṃ naivāsti tathā pūrve 'pi nāstyasau 
anarthe arthasaṃbaddhaṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ pravartate  Lank 
tathatā śūnyatā koṭirnirvāṇaṃ dharmadhātukam 
anutpādaśca dharmāṇāṃ svabhāvaḥ pāramārthikaḥ  Lank 
nāstyastipatitā bālā hetupratyayakalpanaiḥ 
ahetukamanutpannaṃ bhavaṃ vai aprajānataḥ  Lank 
cittaṃ khyāti na dṛśyo 'sti viśeṣo 'nādihetukaḥ 
anādāvapi nāstyartho viśeṣaḥ kena jāyate  Lank 
yadyabhāvena puṣṭiḥ syāddaridro dhanavān bhavet 
arthābhāve kathaṃ cittaṃ jāyate brūhi me mune  Lank 
ahetukamidaṃ sarvaṃ na cittaṃ na ca gocaraḥ 
na ca vai puṣyate cittaṃ tribhavaṃ kriyavarjitam  Lank 
utpādavinivṛttyarthamanutpādaprasādhanam 
ahetuvādaṃ deśemi na ca bālairvibhāvyate 
anutpannamidaṃ sarvaṃ na ca bhāvā na santi ca  Lank 
gandharvasvapnamāyākhyā bhāvā vidyantyahetukāḥ 
anutpannān svabhāvāṃśca śūnyāḥ kena vadāsi me  Lank 
samavāyavinirmukto yadā bhāvo na dṛśyate 
tadā śūnyamanutpannamasvabhāvaṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
svapnakeśoṇḍukaṃ māyā gandharva mṛgatṛṣṇikā 
ahetukā pi dṛśyante tathā lokavicitratā  Lank 
samavāyastathaivaiko dṛśyābhāvānna vidyate 
na tu tīrthyadṛṣṭyā pralayo samavāyo na vidyate  Lank 
vigṛhyāhetuvādena anutpādaṃ prasādhayet 
anutpādaiḥ prasādhyante mama netrī na naśyati  Lank 
ahetuvādairdeśyante tīrthyānāṃ jāyate bhayam 
kathaṃ kena kutaḥ kutra saṃbhavo 'hetuko bhavet  Lank 
Vaidya 
nāhetukamahetutvaṃ yadā paśyanti paṇḍitāḥ 
tadā vyāvartate dṛṣṭirbhaṅgotpādānuvādinī  Lank 
kimabhāvo hyanutpāda utpādotpattilakṣaṇam 
atha bhāvasya nāmedaṃ nirarthaṃ vā bravīhi me  Lank 
na ca bhāvo hyanutpādo na ca pratyayalakṣaṇam 
na ca bhāvasya nāmedaṃ na ca nāma nirarthakam  Lank 
yatra śrāvakabuddhānāṃ tīrthyānāṃ ca agocaraḥ 
saptabhūmigatānāṃ ca tadanutpādalakṣaṇam  Lank 
hetupratyayavyāvṛttiṃ kāraṇasya niṣedhanam 
cittamātravyavasthānamanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
ahetuvṛttiṃ bhāvānāṃ kalpyakalpavivarjitām 
sadasatpakṣanirmuktamanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
cittadṛśyavinirmuktaṃ svabhāvadvayavarjitam 
āśrayasya parāvṛttimanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham  Lank 
na bāhyabhāvaṃ bhāvānāṃ na ca cittaparigraham 
sarvadṛṣṭiprahāṇaṃ yattadanutpādalakṣaṇam  Lank 
evaṃ śūnyāsvabhāvādyān sarvadharmān vibhāvayet 
na jātu śūnyayā śūnyā kiṃ tvanutpādaśūnyayā  Lank 
kalāpaḥ pratyayānāṃ hi pravartate nivartate 
kalapācca pṛthagbhūtaṃ na jātaṃ na nirudhyate  Lank 
bhāvo na vidyate hyanyaḥ kalāpācca pṛthak kvacit 
ekatvena pṛthaktvena yathā tīrthyairvikalpyate  Lank 
sadasanna jāyate bhāvo nāsanna sadasatkvacit 
anyatra hi kalāpo 'yaṃ pravartate nivartate  Lank 
saṃketamātramevedamanyonyāpekṣasaṃkalāt 
janyamarthaṃ na caivāsti pṛthakpratyayasaṃkalāt  Lank 
janyābhāvo hyanutpādaḥ tīrthyadoṣavivarjitaḥ 
deśemi saṃkalāmātraṃ na ca bālairvibhāvyate  Lank 
yasya janyo hi bhāvo 'sti saṃkalāyāḥ pṛthak kvacit 
ahetuvādī vijñeyaḥ saṃkalāyā vināśakaḥ  Lank 
pradīpadravyajātīnāṃ vyañjakā saṃkalā bhavet 
yasya bhāvo bhavetkaścitsaṃkalāyāḥ pṛthak kvacit  Lank 
Vaidya 
asvabhāvo hyanutpannaḥ prakṛtyā gaganopamaḥ 
saṃkalāyāḥ pṛthagbhūto yo dharmaḥ kalpito 'budhaiḥ  Lank 
ayamanyamanutpādamāryāṇāṃ prāptidharmatā 
yaśca tasya anutpādaṃ tadanutpādakṣāntiḥ syāt  Lank 
yadā sarvamimaṃ lokaṃ saṃkalāmeva paśyati 
saṃkalāmātramevedaṃ tadā cittaṃ samādhyate  Lank 
ajñānatṛṣṇākarmādi saṃkalādhyātmikā bhavet 
khajamṛddaṇḍacakrādi bījabhūtādi bāhiram  Lank 
parato yasya vai bhāvaḥ pratyayairjāyate kvacit 
na saṃkalāmātramevedaṃ na te yuktyāgame sthitāḥ  Lank 
yadi janyo na bhāvo 'sti syādbuddhiḥ kasya pratyayāt 
anyonyapratyayā hyete te tena pratyayāḥ smṛtāḥ  Lank 
uṣṇadravacalakaṭhinā bālairdharmā vikalpitāḥ 
kalāpo 'yaṃ na dharmo 'sti ato vai niḥsvabhāvatā  Lank 
vaidyā yathāturavaśātkriyābhedaṃ prakurvate 
na tu śāstrasya bhedo 'sti doṣabhedastu vidyate  Lank 
tathāhaṃ sattvasaṃtāne kleśadoṣaiḥ sudūṣitaiḥ 
indriyāṇāṃ balaṃ jñātvā nayaṃ deśemi bāliśān  Lank 
na kleśendriyabhedena śāsanaṃ bhidyate mama 
ekameva bhavedyānaṃ mārgamaṣṭāṅgikaṃ śivam  Lank 
ghaṭapaṭamukuṭaviṣāṇahetukaśaśaviṣāṇānāstitvam 
yaddhetusamutpannaṃ sa ca nāsti te 'vagantavyam  Lank 
astitvasādhakaṃ nāsti nāsti nāsti na yujyate 
astitvaṃ nāstyapekṣyaṃ hi anyonyāpekṣakāraṇam  Lank 
kiṃcidāśritya punaḥ kiṃcitkhyāyate yasya vai matam 
ahetukaṃ yadāśritya kiṃciccāhetukaṃ na tu  Lank 
atha tadanyamāśritya tadapyanyasya khyāyate 
anavasthā prasajyeta kiṃcicca kiṃ ca no bhavet  Lank 
āśritya parṇakāṣṭhādīn yathā māyā prasajyate 
vastu tadvatsamāśritya vaicitryaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām  Lank 
Vaidya 
māyājālaṃ na parṇāni na kāṣṭhaṃ na ca śarkarā 
māyaiva dṛśyate bālairmāyākāreṇa cāśrayam  Lank 
tathā vastu samāśritya yadi kiṃcidvinaśyati 
dṛśyakāle dvayaṃ nāsti kathaṃ kiṃcidvikalpyate  Lank 
vikalpairvikalpitaṃ nāsti vikalpaśca na vidyate 
vikalpe hyavidyamāne tu na saṃsṛtirna nirvṛtiḥ  Lank 
vikalpe hyavidyamāne tu vikalpo na pravartate 
apravṛttiṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate  Lank 
anekamatibhinnatvācchāsane nāsti sāratā 
sārābhāvānna mokṣo 'sti na ca lokavicitratā  Lank 
bāhyaṃ na vidyate dṛśyaṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate 
bimbavatkhyāyate cittaṃ vāsanairbhramaṇīkṛtam  Lank 
sarvabhāvā hyanutpannā asatsadasaṃbhavāḥ 
cittamātramidaṃ sarvaṃ kalpanābhiśca varjitam  Lank 
bālairbhāvāḥ samākhyātāḥ pratyayairna tu paṇḍitaiḥ 
svabhāvacittanirmuktaścittamāryopagaṃ śivam  Lank 
sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikā nagnā viprāḥ pāśupatāstathā 
asatsaddṛṣṭipatitā viviktārthavivarjitāḥ  Lank 
niḥsvabhāvā hyanutpannāḥ śūnyā māyopamāmalāḥ 
kasyaite deśitā buddhaistvayā ca prativarṇitāḥ  Lank 
yogināṃ śuddhacittānāṃ dṛṣṭitarkavivarjitāḥ 
buddhā deśenti vai yogaṃ mayā ca prativarṇitāḥ  Lank 
yadi cittamidaṃ sarvaṃ kasmiṃllokaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ 
gamanāgamanaṃ kena dṛśyate bhūtale nṛṇām  Lank 
śakuniryathā gagane vikalpena samīritaḥ 
apratiṣṭhamanālambyaṃ carate bhūtale yathā  Lank 
tathā hi dehinaḥ sarve vikalpena samīritāḥ 
svacitte caṃkramante te gagane śukaniryathā  Lank 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ brūhi cittaṃ pravartate 
ābhā vṛttiḥ kathaṃ kena cittamātraṃ vadāhi me  Lank 
dehabhogapratiṣṭhāśca ābhā vṛttiśca vāsanaiḥ 
saṃjāyate ayuktānāmābhā vṛttirvikalpanaiḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
viṣayo vikalpito bhāvaścittaṃ viṣayasaṃbhavam 
dṛśyacittaparijñānādvikalpo na pravartate  Lank 
nāma nāmni visaṃyuktaṃ yadā paśyati kalpitam 
buddhiboddhavyarahitaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ mucyate tadā  Lank 
etā buddhirbhavedbodhyaṃ nāma nāmni vibhāvanam 
ye tvanyathāvabudhyante na te buddhā na bodhakāḥ  Lank 
pañca dharmāḥ svabhāvāśca vijñānānyaṣṭa eva ca 
dve nairātmye bhavetkṛtsno mahāyānaparigrahaḥ  Lank 
yadā buddhiśca boddhavyaṃ viviktaṃ paśyate jagat 
nāsti nāma vikalpaśca tadā nābhipravartate  Lank 
kriyākṣaravikalpānāṃ nivṛttiścittadarśanāt 
adarśanātsvacittasya vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  Lank 
catvāro 'rūpiṇaḥ skandhāḥ saṃkhyā teṣāṃ na vidyate 
bhūtairvilakṣaṇai rūpaṃ kathaṃ rūpabahutvatā  Lank 
lakṣaṇasya parityāgānna bhūtaṃ na ca bhautikam 
athānyalakṣaṇai rūpaṃ kasmātskandhairna jāyate  Lank 
vimuktāyatanaskandhā yadā paśyatyalakṣaṇāḥ 
tadā nivartate cittaṃ dharmanairātmyadarśanāt  Lank 
viṣayendriyabhedena vijñānaṃ jāyate 'ṣṭadhā 
lakṣaṇena bhavetrīṇi nirābhāse nivartate  Lank 
ālayaṃ hi manasyātmā ātmīyaṃ jñānameva ca 
pravartate dvayagrāhātparijñānānnivartate  Lank 
anyānanyavinirmuktaṃ yadā paśyatyasaṃcaram 
tadā dvayaṃ na kalpanti ātmā cātmīyameva ca  Lank 
apravṛttaṃ na puṣṇāti na ca vijñānakāraṇam 
kāryakāraṇanirmuktaṃ niruddhaṃ na pravartate  Lank 
vikalpaṃ cittamātraṃ ca lokaṃ kena vadāhi me 
kāraṇaiśca visaṃyuktaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam  Lank 
svacittaṃ dṛśyate citraṃ dṛśyākāraṃ vikalpitam 
cittadṛśyāparijñānādanyaṃ cittārthasaṃgrahāt  Lank 
Vaidya 
nāstitvadṛṣṭirbhavati yadā buddhyā na paśyati 
astitvaṃ hi kathaṃ tasya cittagrāhānna jāyate  Lank 
vikalpo na bhāvo nābhāvo ato 'stitvaṃ na jāyate 
cittadṛśyaparijñānādvikalpo na pravartate  Lank 
apravṛtti vikalpasya parāvṛtti nirāśrayaḥ 
nivārya pakṣāṃścatvāro yadi bhāvā sahetukāḥ  Lank 
saṃjñāntaraviśeṣo 'yaṃ kṛtaṃ kena na sādhitaḥ 
arthāpattirbhavetteṣāṃ kāraṇādvā pravartate  Lank 
hetupratyayasaṃyogātkāraṇapratiṣedhataḥ 
nityadoṣo nivāryate anityā yadi pratyayāḥ  Lank 
na saṃbhavo na vibhavo anityatvāddhi bāliśām 
na hi naśyamānaṃ kiṃcidvai kāraṇatvena dṛśyate  Lank 
adṛṣṭaṃ hi kathaṃ kena nānityo jāyate bhavaḥ 
saṃgrahaiśca dametsattvān śīlena ca vaśīkaret  Lank 
prajñayā nāśayeddṛṣṭiṃ vimokṣaiśca vivardhayet 
lokāyatamidaṃ sarvaṃ yattīrthyairdeśyate mṛṣā  Lank 
kāryakāraṇasaddṛṣṭyā svasiddhāntaṃ na vidyate 
ahamekaṃ svasiddhāntaṃ kāryakāraṇavarjitaḥ  Lank 
deśemi śiṣyavargasya lokāyatavivarjitaḥ 
cittamātraṃ na dṛśyo 'sti dvidhā cittaṃ vidṛśyate 
grāhyagrāhakabhāvena śāśvatocchedavarjitam  Lank 
yāvatpravartate cittaṃ tāvallokāyataṃ bhavet 
apravṛttirvikalpasya svacittaṃ paśyato jagat  Lank 
āyaṃ kāryābhinirvṛttirvyayaṃ kāryasya darśanam 
āyavyayaparijñānādvikalpo na pravartate  Lank 
nityamanityaṃ kṛtakamakṛtakaṃ parāparam 
evamādyāni sarvāṇi tal
lokāyatanaṃ bhavet  Lank 
devāsuramanuṣyāśca tiryakpretayamālayāḥ 
gatayaḥ ṣaṭ samākhyātā yatra jāyanti dehinaḥ  Lank 
hīnautkṛṣṭamadhyena karmaṇā teṣu jāyate 
saraṃkṣya kuśalān sarvān viśeṣo mokṣa eva vā  Lank 
Vaidya 
kṣaṇe kṣaṇe tvayā yanmaraṇaṃ upapattiṃ ca 
deśyate bhikṣuvargasya abhiprāyaṃ vadāhi me  Lank 
rūpādrūpāntaraṃ yadvaccittaṃ saṃbhūya bhajyate 
tasmāddeśemi śiṣyāṇāṃ kṣaṇajanmaparaṃparām  Lank 
rūpe rūpe vikalpasya saṃbhavo vibhavastathā 
vikalpo hi bhavejjanturvikalpo 'nyo na vidyate  Lank 
kṣaṇe kṣaṇe yanna yuktamidaṃpratyayabhāṣitam 
rūpagrāhavinirmuktaṃ na janma na ca bhajyate  Lank 
pratyayāḥ pratyayotpannā avidyātathatādayaḥ 
dharmadvayena vartante advayā tathatā bhavet  Lank 
pratyayāḥ pratyayotpannā yadi dharmā viśeṣitāḥ 
nityādayo bhavetkāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ pratyayo bhavet  Lank 
nirviśiṣṭaṃ bhavettīrthyaiḥ kāryakāraṇasaṃgrahāt 
vādastava ca buddhānāṃ tasmānnāryo mahāmune  Lank 
śarīre vyāmamātre ca lokaṃ vai lokasamudayam 
nirodhagāminī pratipaddeśayāmi jinaurasān  Lank 
svabhāvatrayagrāheṇa grāhyagrāhavidṛṣṭayaḥ 
lokyalokottarān dharmān vikalpenti pṛthagjanāḥ  Lank 
ataḥ svabhāvagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pūrvapakṣayā 
nivārārthaṃ tu dṛṣṭīnāṃ svabhāvaṃ na vikalpayet  Lank 
chidradoṣānna niyamo na vā cittaṃ pravartate 
pravṛttidvayagrāheṇa advayā tathatā bhavet  Lank 
ajñāna tṛṣṇā karma ca vijñānādyā ayonijāḥ 
anavasthākṛtakatvaṃ ca na kṛtvā jāyate bhavaḥ  Lank 
caturvidhaśca pradhvaṃso bhāvānāṃ kathyate 'budhaiḥ 
dvidhāvṛttervikalpasya bhāvābhāvo na vidyate 
cātuṣkoṭikanirmuktaṃ darśanadvayavarjitam  Lank 
dvidhāvṛttivikalpaḥ syāddṛṣṭvā nābhipravartate 
anutpanneṣu bhāveṣu buddhervyutthānabhāvataḥ  Lank 
utpanneṣvapi bhāveṣu tatkalpatvānna kalpayet 
yuktiṃ vadāhi me nātha dvidhādṛṣṭinivāraṇāt  Lank 
Vaidya 
yathāhamanye ca sadā nāstyasti na visaṃkaret 
tīrthavādaasaṃsṛṣṭāḥ śrāvakairjinavarjitāḥ 
jinābhisamayacaryāṃ ca jinaputrāvināśataḥ  Lank 
vimokṣahetvahetuścāpyanutpādaikalakṣaṇaḥ 
paryāyairmohayantyetāṃ varjanīyāṃ sadā budhaiḥ  Lank 
meghābhrakūṭendradhanuḥprakāśā marīcikeśoṇḍukamāyatulyāḥ 
bhāvā hi sarve svavikalpasaṃbhavāstīrthyā vikalpenti jagatsvakāraṇaiḥ  Lank 
anutpādaśca tathatā bhūtakoṭiśca śūnyatā 
rūpasya nāmānyetāni abhāvaṃ na vikalpayet  Lank 
hastaḥ karo yathā loke indraḥ śakraḥ puraṃdaraḥ 
tathā hi sarvabhāvānāmabhāvaṃ na vikalpayet  Lank 
rūpācca śūnyatā nānyā anutpādaṃ tathaiva ca 
na kalpayedananyatvāddṛṣṭidoṣaḥ prasajyate  Lank 
saṃkalpaśca vikalpaśca vastulakṣaṇasaṃgrahāt 
dīrghahrasvādimāṇḍalyaṃ parikalpasya saṃgrahāt  Lank 
saṃkalpo hi bhaveccittaṃ parikalpo manastathā 
vikalpo manavijñānaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam  Lank 
yacca tīrthyairanutpādo yacca mannayadṛṣṭibhiḥ

prayojanamanutpādamanutpādārthameva ca 
ye vai jānanti yuktijñāste 'bhibudhyanti mannayam  Lank 
prayojanaṃ dṛṣṭisaṃkocamanutpādamanālayam

bhāvā vidyantyanutpannā na vā brūhi mahāmune 
ahetuvādo 'nutpādo pravṛttistīrthadarśanam  Lank 
ahetuvādo 'nutpādo vaiṣamyatīrthadarśanam

utpādamanutpādaṃ varjayeddṛṣṭihetukam 
ahetuvāde 'nutpāde utpāde kāraṇāśrayaḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
anābhogakriyā nāsti kriyā ceddṛṣṭisaṃkaraḥ 
upāyapraṇidhānādyairdṛṣṭimeva vadāhi me 
asattvātsarvadharmāṇāṃ maṇḍalaṃ jāyate katham  Lank 
grāhyagrāhakavisaṃyogānna pravṛttirna nirvṛtiḥ 
bhāvādbhāvāntaraṃ dṛṣṭiṃ cittaṃ vai tatsamutthitam  Lank 
anutpādaśca dharmāṇāṃ kathametadvadāhi me 
sattvāścennāvabudhyante ata etatprakāśyate  Lank 
pūrvottaravirodhaṃ ca sarvaṃ bhāṣya mahāmune 
tīrthadoṣavinirmuktaṃ viṣamāhetuvarjitam  Lank 
apravṛtirnivṛttiśca brūhi me vādināṃvara 
astināstivinirmuktaṃ phalahetvavināśakam  Lank 
bhūmikramānusaṃdhiśca brūhi me dharmalakṣaṇam 
dvayāntapatito loko dṛṣṭibhirvyākulīkṛtaḥ  Lank 
anutpādā utpādādyaiḥ śamaheturna budhyate 
maṇḍalaṃ hi na me kiṃcinna ca deśemi dharmatām  Lank 
dvaye sati hi doṣaḥ syāddvayaṃ buddhairviśodhitam 
śūnyāśca kṣaṇikā bhāvā niḥsvabhāvā hyajātikāḥ  Lank 
kudṛṣṭivādasaṃchannaiḥ kalpyante na tathāgataiḥ 
pravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ ca vikalpasya vadāhi me  Lank 
yathā yena prakāreṇa jāyate viṣayo mukham 
varṇapuṣkalasaṃyogātprapañcaiḥ samudānitam  Lank 
rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā bahirdhā vai vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate 
tasyaiva hi parijñānādyathābhūtārthadarśanāt 
āryagotrānukūlaṃ ca cittaṃ nābhipravartate  Lank 
pratyākhyāya tu bhūtāni bhāvotpattirna vidyate 
bhūtākāraṃ sadā cittamanutpannaṃ vibhāvayet  Lank 
mā vikalpaṃ vikalpetha nirvikalpā hi paṇḍitāḥ 
vikalpaṃ vikalpayaṃstasya dvayameva na nirvṛtiḥ  Lank 
anutpādapratijñasya māyā ca dṛśyate nayaḥ 
māyānirhetusaṃbhūtaṃ hānisiddhāntalakṣaṇam  Lank 
Vaidya 
bimbavaddṛśyate cittamanādimatibhāvitam 
arthākāraṃ na cārtho 'sti yathābhūtaṃ vibhāvayet  Lank 
yathā hi darpaṇe rūpamekatvānyatvavarjitam 
dṛśyate na ca tannāsti tathā cotpādalakṣaṇam  Lank 
gandharvamāyādi yathā hetupratyayalakṣaṇāḥ 
tathā hi sarvabhāvānāṃ saṃbhavo na hyasaṃbhavaḥ  Lank 
vikalpaḥ puruṣākāro dvidhāvṛttyā pravartate 
ātmadharmopacāraiśca na ca bālairvibhāvyate  Lank 
vipulapratyayādhīnaḥ śrāvako 'pi hyarhaṃstathā 
svabalādhīnaṃ jinādhīnaṃ pañcamaṃ śrāvakaṃ nayet  Lank 
kālāntaraṃ ca pradhvastaṃ paramārthetaretaram 
caturvidhamanityatvaṃ bālāḥ kalpentyakovidāḥ  Lank 
dvayāntapatitā bālā guṇāṇuprakṛtikāraṇaiḥ 
mokṣopāyaṃ na jānanti sadasatpakṣasaṃgrahāt  Lank 
aṅgulyagraṃ yathā bālaiścandraṃ gṛhṇanti durmatiḥ 
tathā hyakṣarasaṃsaktāstattvaṃ nāventi māmakam  Lank 
vilakṣaṇāni bhūtāni rūpabhāvapravartakā 
bhūtānāṃ saṃniveśo 'yaṃ na bhūtairbhautikaṃ kṛtam  Lank 
agninā dahyate rūpamabdhātuḥ kledanātmakaḥ 
vāyunā kīryate rūpaṃ kathaṃ bhūtaiḥ pravartate  Lank 
rūpaṃ skandhaśca vijñānaṃ dvayametanna pañcakam 
paryāyabhedaṃ skandhānāṃ śatadhā deśayāmyaham  Lank 
cittacaittasya bhedena vartamānaṃ pravartate 
vyatibhinnāni rūpāṇi cittaṃ rūpaṃ na bhautikam  Lank 
nīlādyapekṣaṇaṃ śvetaṃ śvetaṃ nīlaṃ hyapekṣaṇam 
kāryakāraṇamutpādya śūnyatā asti nāsti ca  Lank 
sādhanaṃ sādhakaṃ sādhyaṃ śītoṣṇe lakṣyalakṣaṇam 
evamādyāni sarvāṇi tārkikairna prasādhitāḥ  Lank 
cittaṃ manaśca ṣaḍvānyavijñānānyātmasaṃyutā 
ekatvānyatvarahitā ālayo 'yaṃ pravartate  Lank 
sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikā nagnāstārkikā īśvaroditāḥ 
sadasatpakṣapatitā viviktārthavivarjitāḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
saṃsthānākṛtiviśeṣo bhūtānāṃ nāsti bhautikam 
tīrthyā vadanti janma bhūtānāṃ bhautikasya ca  Lank 
anutpannā yato ye 'nye tīrthyāḥ kalpanti kāraṇaiḥ 
na ca budhyanti mohena sadasatpakṣamāśritāḥ  Lank 
cittena saha saṃyuktaṃ visaṃyuktaṃ manādibhiḥ 
viśuddhalakṣaṇaṃ sattvaṃ jñānena saha tiṣṭhati  Lank 
karma yacca bhavedrūpaṃ skandhaviṣayahetukāḥ 
sattvāśca nirupādānā ārūpye nāvatiṣṭhati  Lank 
nairātmyaṃ sattvavāditvaṃ sattvābhāvātprasajyate 
nairātmyavādino cchedo vijñānasyāpyasaṃbhavaḥ  Lank 
catvāraḥ sthitastasya rūpābhāvātkathaṃ bhavet 
adhyātmabāhyābhāvādvijñānaṃ na pravartate  Lank 
antarābhavikāḥ skandhāḥ yathaivecchanti tārkikāḥ 
tathārūpyopapannasya bhavo 'rūpo na cāsti kim  Lank 
aprayatnena mokṣaḥ syātsattvavijñānayorvinā 
tīrthyavādo na saṃdeho na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ  Lank 
rūpaṃ ca vidyate tatra ārūpye nāsti darśanam 
tadabhāvo na siddhānto na yānaṃ na ca yāyinam  Lank 
indriyaiḥ saha saṃyuktaṃ vijñānaṃ vāsanodbhavam 
aṣṭavidhaikadeśaṃ hi kṣaṇe kāle na gṛhṇanti  Lank 
na pravartati yadā rūpaṃ indriyā na ca indriyaiḥ 
ato hi deśeti bhagavān kṣaṇikā indriyādayaḥ  Lank 
anirdhārya kathaṃ rūpaṃ vijñānaṃ saṃpravartsyate 
apravṛttaṃ kathaṃ jñānaṃ saṃsāraṃ janayiṣyati  Lank 
utpattyanantaraṃ bhaṅgaṃ na deśenti vināyakāḥ 
nairantaryaṃ na bhāvānāṃ vikalpaspandite gatau  Lank 
indriyā indriyārthāśca mūḍhānāṃ na tu paṇḍitāḥ 
bālā gṛhṇanti nāmena āryā vai arthakovidāḥ  Lank 
ṣaṣṭhaṃ hi nirupādānaḥ sopādāno na gṛhyate 
anirdhāryaṃ vadantyāryāṃ astidoṣairvivarjitāḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
śāśvatocchedabhītāśca tārkikā jñānavarjitāḥ 
saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtātmānaṃ na viśeṣanti bāliśāḥ  Lank 
ekatve vidyate dānamanyatve cāpi vidyate 
cittena saha caikatvamanyatvaṃ vai manādibhiḥ  Lank 
nirdhāryate yadā dānaṃ cittaṃ caittābhiśabditam 
upādānātkathaṃ tatra ekatvenāvadhāryate  Lank 
sopādānopalabdhiśca karmajanmakriyādibhiḥ 
agnivatsādhayiṣyanti sadṛśāsadṛśairnaryaiḥ  Lank 
yathā hi agniryugapaddahyate dāhyadāhakau 
sopādānastathā hyātmā tārkikaiḥ kiṃ na gṛhyate  Lank 
utpādādvāpyanutpādāccittaṃ vai bhāsvaraṃ sadā 
dṛṣṭāntaṃ kiṃ na kurvanti tārkikā ātmasādhakāḥ  Lank 
vijñānagahvare mūḍhāstārkikā nayavarjitāḥ 
itastataḥ pradhāvanti ātmavādacikīrṣayā  Lank 
pratyātmagatigamyaśca ātmā vai śuddhilakṣaṇam 
garbhastathāgatasyāsau tārkikāṇāmagocaraḥ  Lank 
upādānaupādātrorvibhāgaskandhayostathā 
lakṣaṇaṃ yadi jānāti jñānaṃ saṃjāyate nayam  Lank 
ālayaṃ garbhasaṃsthānaṃ mataṃ tīrthyānuvarṇitam 
ātmanā saha saṃyuktaṃ na ca dharmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  Lank 
eteṣāṃ pravibhāgena vimokṣaḥ satyadarśanam 
bhāvānāṃ darśyaheyānāṃ kleśānāṃ syādviśodhanam  Lank 
prakṛtiprabhāsvaraṃ cittaṃ garbhaṃ tāthāgataṃ śubham 
upādānaṃ hi sattvasya antānantavivarjitam  Lank 
kāntiryathā suvarṇasya jātarūpaṃ ca śarkaram 
parikarmeṇa paśyanti sattvaṃ skandhālayaistathā  Lank 
na pudgalo na ca skandhā buddho jñānamanāsravam 
sadāśāntiṃ vibhāvitvā gacchāmi śaraṇaṃ hyaham  Lank 
prakṛtiprabhāsvaraṃ cittamupakleśairmanādibhiḥ 
ātmanā saha saṃyuktaṃ deśeti vadatāṃvaraḥ  Lank 
prakṛtiprabhāsvaraṃ cittaṃ manādyastasya vai paraḥ 
tairācitāni karmāṇi yataḥ kliśyanti tāvubhau  Lank 
Vaidya 
āgantukairānādyaiśca kleśairātmā prabhāsvaraḥ 
saṃkliśyate upetaśca vastravatpariśudhyate  Lank 
malābhāvādyathā vastraṃ hemaṃ vā doṣavarjitam 
tiṣṭhanti na ca naśyante ātmā doṣaistathā vinā  Lank 
vīṇāśaṅkhe 'tha bheryāṃ ca mādhuryasvarasaṃpadā 
mṛgayeddhyakovidaḥ kaścittathā skandheṣu pudgalam  Lank 
nidhayo maṇayaścāpi pṛthivyāmudakaṃ tathā 
vidyamānā na dṛśyanti tathā skandheṣu pudgalam  Lank 
cittacaittakalāpāṃśca svaguṇāṃ skandhasaṃyutāṃ 
akovidā na gṛhṇanti tathā skandheṣu pudgalam  Lank 
yathā hi garbho garbhiṇyāṃ vidyate na ca dṛśyate 
ātmā hi tadvatskandheṣu ayuktijño na paśyati  Lank 
auṣadhīnāṃ yathā sāramagniṃ vā indhanairyathā 
na paśyanti ayuktijñāstathā skandheṣu pudgalam  Lank 
anityatāṃ sarvabhāveṣu śūnyatāṃ ca yathābudhāḥ 
vidyamānāṃ na paśyanti tathā skandheṣu pudgalam  Lank 
bhūmayo vaśitābhijñā abhiṣekaṃ ca uttaram 
samādhayo viśeṣāśca asatyātmani nāsti vai  Lank 
vaināśiko yadā gatvā brūyādyadyasti deśyatām 
sa vaktavyo bhavedvijñaḥ svavikalpaṃ pradarśaya  Lank 
nairātmyavādino 'bhāṣyā bhikṣukarmāṇi varjaya 
bādhakā buddhadharmāṇāṃ sadasatpakṣadṛṣṭayaḥ  Lank 
tīrthadoṣairvinirmuktaṃ nairātmyavanadāhakam 
jājvalatyātmavādo 'yaṃ yugāntāgnirivotthitaḥ  Lank 
khaṇḍekṣuśarkaramadhvādidadhitilaghṛtādiṣu 
svarasaṃ vidyate teṣu anāsvādyaṃ na gṛhyate  Lank 
pañcadhā gṛhyamāṇaśca ātmā skandhasamucchraye 
na ca paśyantyavidvāṃso vidvān dṛṣṭvā vimucyate  Lank 
vidyādibhiśca dṛṣṭāntaiścittaṃ naivāvadhāryate 
yatra yasmādyadarthaṃ ca samūhaṃ nāvadhāryate  Lank 
vilakṣaṇā hi vai dharmāścittamekaṃ na gṛhyate 
aheturapravṛttiśca tārkikāṇāṃ prasajyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
cittānupaśyī ca yogī cittaṃ citte na paśyati 
paśyako dṛśyanirjāto dṛśyaṃ kiṃ hetusaṃbhavam  Lank 
kātyāyanasya gotro 'haṃ śuddhāvāsādviniḥsṛtaḥ 
deśemi dharmaṃ sattvānāṃ nirvāṇapuragāminam  Lank 
paurāṇikamidaṃ vartma ahaṃ te ca tathāgatāḥ 
tribhiḥ sahasraiḥ sūtrāṇāṃ nirvāṇamatyadeśayan  Lank 
kāmadhātau tathārūpye na vai buddho vibudhyate 
rūpadhātvakaniṣṭheṣu vītarāgeṣu budhyate  Lank 
na bandhaheturviṣayā heturviṣayabandhanam 
jñānabadhyāni kleśāni asidhāravrato hyayam  Lank 
asatyātmani māyādyā dharmā nāstyasti vai katham 
bālānāṃ khyāti tathatā kathaṃ nāsti nirātmikā  Lank 
kṛtakākṛtakatvāddhi nāsti hetuḥ pravartakaḥ 
anutpannamidaṃ sarvaṃ na ca bālairvibhāvyate  Lank 
kāraṇāni anutpannā kṛtakāḥ pratyayāśca te 
dvāvapyetau na janakau kāraṇaiḥ kalpyate katham  Lank 
prākpaścādyugapaccāpi hetuṃ varṇenti tārkikāḥ 
prakāśaghaṭaśiṣyādyairbhāvānāṃ janma kathyate  Lank 
nābhisaṃskārikairbuddhā lakṣaṇairlakṣaṇānvitāḥ 
cakravartiguṇā hyete naite buddhaprabhāṣitāḥ  Lank 
buddhānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ dṛṣṭidoṣairvivarjitam 
pratyātmadṛṣṭigatikaṃ sarvadoṣavighātakam  Lank 
badhirāndhakāṇamūkānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ vairavṛttinām 
bālānāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa brahmacaryaṃ na vidyate  Lank 
āvṛtairvyañjanairdivyairlakṣaṇaiścakravartinaḥ 
vyañjitaiḥ pravrajantyeke na cānye ca pravādinaḥ  Lank 
vyāsaḥ kaṇādaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ kapilaḥ śākyanāyakaḥ 
nirvṛte mama paścāttu bhaviṣyantyevamādayaḥ  Lank 
mayi nirvṛte varṣaśate vyāso vai bhāratastathā 
pāṇḍavāḥ kauravā rāmaḥ paścānmaurī bhaviṣyati  Lank 
mauryā nandāśca guptāśca tato mlecchā nṛpādhamāḥ 
mlecchānte śastrasaṃkṣobhaḥ śastrānte ca kaliryugaḥ 
kaliyugānte lokaiśca saddharmo hi na bhāvitaḥ  Lank 
Vaidya 
evamādyānyatītāni cakravadbhramate jagat 
vahnyādityasamāyogātkāmadhāturvidīryate  Lank 
punaḥ saṃsthāsyate divyaṃ tasmiṃllokaḥ pravartsyate 
cātuṃ rvarṇā nṛpendrāśca ṛṣayo dharmameva ca  Lank 
vedāśca yajñaṃ dānaṃ ca dharmasthā vartsyate punaḥ 
ākhyāyiketihāsādyairgadyacūrṇikavārtikaiḥ 
evaṃ mayā śrutādibhyo loko vai vibhramiṣyati  Lank 
suraktākoṭitaṃ kṛtvā upariṣṭādvivarṇayet 
nīlakardamagomayaiḥ paṭaṃ vai saṃpracitrayet 
sarvavāsairvicitrāṅgastīrthyaliṅgavivarjitaḥ  Lank 
śāsanaṃ deśayedyogī buddhānāmeṣa vai dhvajaḥ 
vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ peyaṃ kaṭisūtraṃ ca dhārayet 
upapadyamānaṃ kālena bhaikṣyaṃ vā nīcavarjitam  Lank 
divyaṃ saṃjāyate svargāddvau cānyau mānuṣodbhavau 
ratnalakṣaṇasaṃpanno devajanmajageśvaraḥ  Lank 
svargaṃ prabhuñjate dvīpāṃścaturo dharmaśāsanaḥ 
bhuktvā tu suciraṃ dvīpāṃstṛṣṇayā vipraṇaśyati  Lank 
kṛtayugaśca tretā ca dvāparaṃ kalinastathā 
ahaṃ cānye kṛtayuge śākyasiṃhaḥ kalau yuge  Lank 
siddhārthaḥ śākyatanayo viṣṇurvyāso maheśvaraḥ 
evamādyāni tīrthyāni nirvṛte me bhaviṣyati  Lank 
evaṃ mayā śrutādibhyaḥ śākyasiṃhasya deśanā 
itihāsaṃ purāvṛttaṃ vyāsasyaitadbhaviṣyati  Lank 
viṣṇurmaheśvaraścāpi sṛṣṭitvaṃ deśayiṣyati 
evaṃ me nirvṛte paścādevamādyaṃ bhaviṣyati  Lank 
mātā ca me vasumatiḥ pitā vipraḥ prajāpatiḥ 
kātyāyanasagotro 'haṃ nāmnā vai virajo jinaḥ  Lank 
campāyāṃ haṃ samutpannaḥ pitāpi ca pitāmahaḥ 
somagupteti nāmnāsau somavaṃśasamudbhavaḥ  Lank 
cīrṇavrataḥ pravrajitaḥ sahasraṃ deśitaṃ nayam 
vyākṛtya parinirvāsye abhiṣicya mahāmatim  Lank 
Vaidya 
matirdāsyati dharmāya dharmo dāsyati mekhale 
mekhalaḥ śiṣyo daurbalyātkalpānte nāśayiṣyati  Lank 
kāśyapaḥ krakucchandaśca kanakaśca vināyakaḥ 
ahaṃ ca virajo 'nye vai sarve te kṛtino jināḥ  Lank 
kṛte yuge tataḥ paścānmatirnāmena nāyakaḥ 
bhaviṣyati mahāvīraḥ pañcajñeyāvabodhakaḥ  Lank 
na dvāpare na tretāyāṃ na paścācca kalau yuge 
saṃbhavo lokanāthānāṃ saṃbudhyante kṛte yuge  Lank 
ahāryā lakṣaṇāyāśca acchinnadaśakaiḥ saha 
moracandrasamaiścandrairuttarīyaṃ vicitrayet  Lank 
dvayaṅgulaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ vāpi candraṃ candrāntaraṃ bhavet 
anyathā citryamānaṃ hi lobhanīyaṃ hi bāliśān  Lank 
rāgāgniṃ śamayennityaṃ snāyādvai jñānavāriṇā 
triśaraṇaṃ trisaṃdhyāsu yogī kuryātprayatnataḥ  Lank 
iṣuprastarakāṣṭhādyā utkṣepādyaiḥ samīritāḥ 
ekaḥ kṣiptaḥ patatyekaḥ kuśalākuśalastathā  Lank 
ekaṃ ca bahudhā nāsti vailakṣaṇyānna kutracit 
vāyubhā grāhakāḥ sarve kṣetravaddāyakā bhavet  Lank 
yadyekaṃ bahudhā vai syātsarve hyakṛtakā bhavet 
kṛtakasya vināśaḥ syāttārkikāṇāmayaṃ nayaḥ  Lank 
dīpabījavadetatsyātsādṛśyādbahudhā kutaḥ 
ekaṃ hi bahudhā bhavati tārkikāṇāmayaṃ nayaḥ  Lank 
na tilājjāyate mudgo na vrīhiryavahetukaḥ 
godhūmadhānyajātāni ekaṃ hi bahudhā katham  Lank 
pāṇiniṃ śabdanetāramakṣapādo bṛhaspatiḥ 
lokāyatapraṇetāro brahmā garbho bhaviṣyati  Lank 
kātyāyanaḥ sūtrakartā yajñavalkastathaiva ca 
bhuḍhukajyotiṣādyāni bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge  Lank 
balī puṇyakṛtāllokātprajābhāgyādbhaviṣyati 
rakṣakaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ rājā balī mahīpatiḥ  Lank 
vālmīko masurākṣaśca kauṭilya āśvalāyanaḥ 
ṛṣayaśca mahābhāgā bhaviṣyanti anāgate  Lank 
Vaidya 
siddhārthaḥ śākyatanayo bhūtāntaḥ pañcacūḍakaḥ 
vāgbaliratha medhāvī paścātkāle bhaviṣyati  Lank 
ajinaṃ daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ ca mekhalācakramaṇḍalam 
dadāti brahmā maheśvaro vanabhūmau vyavasthite  Lank 
bhaviṣyati mahāyogī nāmnā vai virajo muniḥ 
mokṣasya deśakaḥ śāstā munīnāmeṣa vai dhvajaḥ  Lank 
brahmā brahmaśataiḥ sārdhaṃ devaiśca bahubhirmama 
ajinaṃ prapātya gaganāttatraivāntarhito vaśī  Lank 
sarvacitrāṇi vāsāṃsi bhaikṣyapātraṃ suraiḥ saha 
indro virūḍhakādyāśca vanabhūmau dadanti me  Lank 
anutpādavādahetviṣṭo 'jāto jāyeta vā punaḥ 
sādhayiṣyatyanutpādaṃ vāṅbhātraṃ kīrtyate tu vai  Lank 
tasyāvidyā kāraṇaṃ teṣāṃ cittānāṃ saṃpravartitā 
antarā kimavasthāsau yāvadrūpaṃ na jānati  Lank 
samanantarapradhvastaṃ cittamanyatpravartate 
rūpaṃ na tiṣṭhate kiṃcitkimālambya pravartsyate  Lank 
yasmādyatra pravarteta cittaṃ vitathahetukam 
na prasiddhaṃ kathaṃ tasya kṣaṇabhaṅgo 'vadhāryate  Lank 
yogināṃ hi samāpattiḥ suvarṇajinadhātavaḥ 
ābhāsvaravimānāni abhedyā lokakāraṇāt  Lank 
sthitayaḥ prāptidharmāśca buddhānāṃ jñānasaṃpadaḥ 
bhikṣutvaṃ samayaprāptirdṛṣṭā vai kṣaṇikā katham  Lank 
gandharvapuramāyādyā rūpā vai kṣaṇikā katham 
abhūtikā ca bhūtāni bhūtāḥ kiṃcitkva cāgatau  Lank 
avidyāhetukaṃ cittamanādimatisaṃcitam 
utpādabhaṅgasaṃbaddhaṃ tārkikaiḥ saṃprakalpyate  Lank 
dvividhaḥ sāṃkhyavādaśca pradhānātpariṇāmikam 
pradhāne vidyate kāryaṃ kāryaṃ svātmaprasādhitam  Lank 
pradhānaṃ saha bhāvena guṇabhedaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
kāryakāraṇavaicitryaṃ pariṇāme na vidyate  Lank 
yathā hi pāradaḥ śuddha upakleśairna lipyate 
ālayaṃ hi tathā śuddhamāśrayaḥ sarvadehinām  Lank 
Vaidya 
hiṅgugandhaḥ palāṇḍuśca garbhiṇyā garbhadarśanam 
lavaṇādibhiśca lāvaṇyaṃ bījavatkiṃ na vartate  Lank 
anyatve ca tadanyatve ubhayaṃ nobhaye tathā 
astitvaṃ nirupādānaṃ na ca nāsti na saṃskṛtam  Lank 
aśvavadvidyate hyātmā skandhairgobhāvavarjitam 
saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtaṃ vācyamavaktavyaṃ svabhāvakam  Lank 
yuktyāgamābhyāṃ durdṛṣṭyā tarkadṛṣṭyā malīkṛtam 
anirdhāryaṃ vadantyātmā nopādāne na cānyataḥ  Lank 
doṣanirdhāraṇā hyeṣāṃ skandhenātmā vibhāvyate 
ekatvena tadanyatvena na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ  Lank 
darpaṇe udake netre yatha bimbaṃ pradṛśyate 
ekatvānyatvarahitastathā skandheṣu pudgalaḥ  Lank 
bhāvyaṃ vibhāvanādhyātā mārgaḥ satyā ca darśanam 
etatrayaṃ vibhāvento mucyante hi kudarśanaiḥ  Lank 
dṛṣṭaṃ naṣṭaṃ yathā vidyuccakraṃ chidragṛhe yathā 
pariṇāmaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ bālairiva na kalpayet  Lank 
bhāvābhāvena nirvāṇaṃ bālānāṃ cittamohanam 
āryadarśanasadbhāvādyathāvasthānadarśanāt  Lank 
utpādabhaṅgarahitaṃ bhāvābhāvavivarjitam 
lakṣyalakṣaṇanirmuktaṃ pariṇāmaṃ vibhāvayet  Lank 
tīrthyavādavinirmuktaṃ nāmasaṃsthānavarjitam 
adhyātmadṛṣṭinilayaṃ pariṇāmaṃ vibhāvayet  Lank 
saṃsparśapīḍanābhyāṃ vai devānāṃ nārakāṇi ca 
antarābhavikā nāsti vijñānena pravartitā  Lank 
jarajāṇḍajasaṃsvedādyā antarābhavasaṃbhavāḥ 
sattvakāyā yathā citrā gatyāgatyāṃ vibhāvayet  Lank 
yuktyāgamavyapetāni niḥkleśapakṣakṣayāvahā 
tīrthyadṛṣṭipralāpāni matimānna samācaret  Lank 
ādau nirdhāryate ātmā upādānādviśeṣayet 
anirdhārya viśeṣanti vandhyāputraṃ viśiṣyate  Lank 
paśyāmi sattvān divyena prajñāmāṃsavivarjitam 
saṃsāraskandhanirmuktaṃ mūrtimān sarvadehinām  Lank 
Vaidya 
durvarṇasuvarṇagataṃ muktāmuktaviśeṣaṇam 
divyaṃ saṃskāravigataṃ saṃskārasthaṃ prapaśyate  Lank 
mūrtimān gatisaṃdhau vai tārkikāṇāmagocaram 
atikrāntamānuṣyagatimahaṃ nānye kutārkikāḥ  Lank 
nāstyātmā jāyate cittaṃ kasmādetatpravartate 
nadīdīpabījavattasya nirgamaḥ kiṃ na kathyate  Lank 
anutpanne ca vijñāne ajñānādi na vidyate 
tadabhāve na vijñānaṃ saṃtatyā jāyate katham  Lank 
adhvatrayamanadhvaśca avaktavyaśca pañcamaḥ 
jñeyametaddhi buddhānāṃ tārkikaiḥ saṃprakīrtyate  Lank 
avaktavyaśca saṃskārairjñānaṃ saṃskārahetukam 
gṛhṇāti saṃskāragataṃ jñānaṃ saṃskāraśabditam  Lank 
asmin satīdaṃ bhavati pratyayāścāpyahetukāḥ 
vyañjakenopadiśyante tadabhāvānna kārakam  Lank 
pavanaṃ hi vahnerdahanaṃ preraṇe na tu saṃbhave 
prerya nirvāyate tena kathaṃ sattvaprasādhakāḥ  Lank 
saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtaṃ vācyamupādānavivarjitam 
kathaṃ hi sādhakastasya vahnirbālairvikalpyate  Lank 
anyonyasya balādhānādvahnirvai jāyate nṛṇām 
sattvaḥ pravartitaḥ kena vahnivatkalpyate yataḥ  Lank 
skandhāyatanakadambasya manādyākāraṇo nu vai 
nairātmā sārthavannityaṃ cittena saha vartate  Lank 
dvāvetau bhāsvarau nityaṃ kāryakāraṇavarjitau 
agnirhyasādhakasteṣāṃ na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ  Lank 
cittaṃ sattvāśca nirvāṇaṃ prakṛtyā bhāsurā nu vai 
doṣairanādikaiḥ kliṣṭā abhinnā gaganopamāḥ  Lank 
hastiśayyādivacchāyā
stīrthyadṛṣṭyā malīkṛtāḥ 
manovijñānasaṃchannā agnirādyairviśodhitāḥ  Lank 
dṛṣṭāśca te yathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā kleśā vidāritāḥ 
dṛṣṭāntagahanaṃ hitvā gatāste āryagocaram  Lank 
jñānajñeyavibhāgena anyatvaṃ kalpyate yataḥ 
na ca budhyanti durmedhā avaktavyaśca kathyate  Lank 
Vaidya 
bherī yathā candanajā bālaiḥ kurvanti nānyathā 
candanāgarusaṃkāśaṃ tathā jñānaṃ kutārkikaiḥ  Lank 
utthitaḥ khalubhaktaśca pātrasaṃśritamātrakam 
doṣairmukhavikārādyaiḥ śuddhaṃ bhaktaṃ samācaret  Lank 
imaṃ nayaṃ yo 'numinoti yuktitaḥ prasādavān yogaparo hyakalpanaḥ 
anāśrito hyarthaparo bhavedasau hiraṇmayīṃ dharmagatiṃ pradīpayet  Lank 
bhāvābhāvapratyayamohakalpanā kudṛṣṭijālaṃ samalaṃ hi tasya tu 
sarāgadoṣapratighaṃ nivartate nirañjano buddhakaraiśca sicyate  Lank 
tīrthyā kāraṇadigmūḍhā anye pratyayavihvalāḥ 
anye ahetusadbhāvāducchedaṃ āryamāsthitāḥ  Lank 
vipākapariṇāmaśca vijñānasya manasya ca 
mano hyālayasaṃbhūtaṃ vijñānaṃ ca manobhavam  Lank 
ālayātsarvacittāni pravartanti taraṃgavat 
vāsanāhetukāḥ sarve yathāpratyayasaṃbhavāḥ  Lank 
kṣaṇabhedasaṃkalābaddhāḥ svacittārthavigrāhiṇaḥ 
saṃsthānalakṣaṇākārā manocakṣvādisaṃbhavāḥ  Lank 
anādidoṣasaṃbaddhamarthābhāvāsanoditam 
bahirdhā dṛśyate cittaṃ tīrthadṛṣṭinivāraṇam  Lank 
taddhetukamevānyattadālambya pravartate 
yadā saṃjāyate dṛṣṭiḥ saṃsāraśca pravartate  Lank 
māyāsvapnanibhā bhāvā gandharvanagaropamāḥ 
marīcyudakacandrābhāḥ svavikalpaṃ vibhāvayet  Lank 
vṛttibhedāttu tathatā samyagjñānaṃ tadāśrayam 
māyāśūraṃgamādīni samādhīni parāṇi ca  Lank 
bhūmipraveśāllabhate abhijñā vaśitāni ca 
jñānamāyopamaṃ kāyamabhiṣiktaṃ ca saugatam  Lank 
nivartate yadā cittaṃ nivṛttaṃ paśyato jagat 
muditāṃ labhate bhūmiṃ buddhabhūmiṃ labhanti ca  Lank 
Vaidya 
āśrayeṇa nivṛttena viśvarūpo maṇiryathā 
karoti sattvakṛtyāni pratibimbaṃ yathā jale  Lank 
sadasatpakṣanirmuktamubhayaṃ nobhayaṃ na ca 
pratyekaśrāvakīyābhyāṃ niṣkrāntā saptamī bhavet  Lank 
pratyātmadṛṣṭadharmāṇāṃ bhūtabhūmiviśodhitam 
bāhyatīrthyavinirmuktaṃ mahāyānaṃ vinirdiśet  Lank 
parāvṛttirvikalpasya cyutināśavivarjitam 
śaśaromamaṇiprakhyaṃ muktānāṃ deśayennayam  Lank 
yathā hi grantho granthena yuktyā yuktistathā yadi 
ato yuktirbhavedyuktimanyathā tu na kalpayet  Lank 
cakṣuḥ karma ca tṛṣṇā ca avidyāyoniśastathā 
cakṣūrūpe manaścāpi āvilasya manastathā  Lank 
ityāryasaddharmalaṅkāvatāro nāma mahāyānasūtraṃ sagāthakaṃ samāptamiti 
ye dharmā hetuprabhavā hetuṃ teṣāṃ tathāgato hyavadat 
teṣāṃ ca yo nirodho evaṃ vādī mahāśramaṇaḥ
